Current Affairs Commentary

British Mediation of the Italian-Ethiopian Dispute 23

— Heng

Britain has dispatched Eden to Italy to mediate the Italian-Ethiopian dispute, this being the second time. The result of the previous mediation was that Italy and Ethiopia would organize an arbitration committee in accordance with the 1928 Treaty of Friendship to resolve the dispute, with a deadline of August 25th this year to complete the solution. If no agreement is reached by then, the League of Nations Administrative Council will handle the matter. However, since Eden's return to England, Mussolini has continued to increase troops in East Africa while repeatedly issuing statements that do not allow third-party interference. At the same time, the Italian newspapers are unanimously attacking England. Judging from the intense emotions of the Italian government and people, it can be seen that Italy fundamentally does not want to abandon its ambition to seize Ethiopia. The reason why it temporarily accepted Eden's mediation plan is probably to give England face. Now that the Anglo-German naval agreement has been established, and cracks have appeared in the Anglo-French-Italian front against Germany, Italy can barely contain its anger towards England. Britain seeks Italy's understanding at this time, fearing it might be too late. Now it wants to mediate the Italian-Ethiopian dispute again. The difficulty of this matter will certainly be even greater than Eden's previous trip to Rome.

The most difficult aspect of Britain's mediation of the Italian-Ethiopian dispute is the issue of the League of Nations' credibility. Although Abyssinia is an African country, it is also a member of the League of Nations. According to the charter, other member states should not infringe on its territorial integrity and sovereign independence. Moreover, Britain has always claimed to be upholding the League of Nations' credibility in its past interventions in Italy. How can it now suddenly undermine its position to show goodwill to the Italians? Therefore, judging from this point, even if the British want to make concessions to Italy, they may not be able to come up with a plan that does not harm the League of Nations' credibility, so as to satisfy Italy's desires. According to recent telegrams, Eden's mediation plan is to allow Italy to build a railway through Ethiopian territory to connect Italian Somaliland and Eritrea. For Ethiopia, Britain would allow it to use British Somaliland ports to the Red Sea as compensation. This is truly a way to save face for both Italy and Ethiopia, while not putting the League of Nations in a hopeless situation. However, Mussolini insists on fundamentally changing the Ethiopian political system and has rejected the above mediation plan. Therefore, in order to gain Italy's favor and achieve its goal of stabilizing the European situation, Britain may have to reconsider the Ethiopian issue.

Sir Otto Niemeyer to Arrive in China in August Via the United States - Various Circles Observe the Mission of Niemeyer's Trip as a Manifestation of Britain's Active Far East Policy 24

(London) British financial expert Sir Otto Niemeyer plans to depart for China on August 10th. The route has not yet been decided, but it is widely believed that Niemeyer will travel via the United States and arrive in Shanghai around the second week of September. Niemeyer is currently studying Chinese affairs. Business and political circles are paying increasing attention to Niemeyer's mission, recognizing that Niemeyer's trip is a concrete manifestation of the British government's intention to adopt an active policy in the Far East. However, this move is not intended to be anti-Japanese, nor is it hostile to Japan's natural interests, but rather an effort to seek cooperation for the common benefit and peace of the Far East. (27th, Reuter's Dispatch)

Shih Chao-chi Appointed Ambassador to the United States - Washington Newspaper Expresses Delight 25

(Washington) The Washington Star stated in an editorial today that the United States is very pleased with the appointment of Shih Chao-chi as China's first ambassador to the United States. The newspaper detailed Shih's scholarship and experience, and said, "The United States has always paid attention to the welfare of China, and the factual manifestations are too numerous to mention. Shih has been instrumental in maintaining this friendship between the United States and China," etc. (26th, National Dispatch)

Few Achievements in British Diplomacy - Eden Returns Home Via Paris - Holds Another Meeting with Laval - Seeking a Way to Reconcile Differences 26

(Paris) Minister Without Portfolio Eden and his entourage arrived here from Rome at 10:05 this morning. They held talks at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs with Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval and French experts until 1:30 PM. According to an official communique, the talks today only discussed how to find the best way to reconcile the methods used by the two governments to implement the various procedures contained in the London Declaration of February 3rd. The British government advocates that the various security organization issues be negotiated and handled separately, while the French government advocates joint handling. A way to adjust the two must be sought. It is heard that this issue will be discussed further by the British and French governments through diplomatic negotiations. (27th, Havas Dispatch)

(Paris) After returning here from Rome today, Eden immediately met with French Prime Minister Laval for two hours. Although no concrete decisions were made, progress has been made on finding a common position to adjust the methods by which the British and French governments implement the procedures outlined in the London Declaration of February 2nd. It is widely believed that Eden informed Laval of his meeting with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini regarding the Italian-Ethiopian dispute. Eden is scheduled to depart for London this afternoon. (27th, Reuter's Dispatch)

The Ethiopian Question - British Mediation Ultimately Fails - Italy Intends to Reduce Ethiopia to a Protectorate - Peace in East Africa Hanging by a Thread 27

(London) According to reliable sources here, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini has expressed to British Minister Without Portfolio Eden during yesterday's talks that he will reject Britain's proposal and demand important rights from Ethiopia. It is heard that Mussolini has demanded that Ethiopia become a protectorate, with Italy having the right to station officials in the Ethiopian capital. From this point of view, Britain's mediation has obviously completely failed. At the same time, Italy has entered a state where war could break out at any time. Officials also acknowledge that the crisis of war is very serious. News from the Ethiopian side here is that Ethiopia is also preparing to defend its territory and is willing to fight if necessary. (26th, National Dispatch)

British Newspapers Worry About the Future - Italy May Challenge the League of Nations - The Seriousness Is No Less Than the Manchurian Incident 28

(London) Italian Prime Minister Mussolini's expression of stern demands for a thorough solution to the Italian-Ethiopian dispute, as a permanent solution, has caused alarm in all the newspapers this morning. It is believed that Eden will realize during his reunion with French Prime Minister Laval in Paris that war in North Africa cannot be avoided this autumn, and that Italy may challenge the League of Nations. Its seriousness should be no less than Japan's handling of the Manchurian issue. The diplomatic correspondent of the Morning Post said that Italy cannot be satisfied unless Abyssinia is made an informal protectorate of Italy. Italy's current goal is to build a railway to connect Eritrea with Italian Somaliland facing Asab. Since the Italian Prime Minister explained his position on these points, Eden no longer presented the British mediation proposal to him. The British Cabinet meeting yesterday viewed this result as a serious development. The Daily Telegraph said that the Italians now intend to make Abyssinia a protectorate of the Italian army, with everything done in the manner of Morocco, and Emperor Selassie in the position of a puppet. Only then can the situation in Northeast Africa be resolved. At the same time, Italy's war preparations in Northeast Africa are still actively underway. In the past few weeks, regular troops have regularly departed from Cagliari. The final two divisions of Blackshirts to be mobilized are undergoing rigorous training in Naples and will soon depart as well. (27th, Reuter's Dispatch)

Ingenious Plan Rejected by Italy 29

(London) It has been learned here that Mussolini did not accept any of the points of peace appealed by Eden, British Minister for League of Nations Affairs, during the talks in Rome. Eden claimed that if Italy goes to war with Ethiopia, the policy of cooperation between Britain, France and Italy on the European political situation will inevitably be hit. Furthermore, if Italy, as a member of the League of Nations, adopts the means of war against another member state, what a blow this will be to international relations. It is known that the concessions Britain has persuaded Ethiopia to make are twofold: one is to increase Italy's business opportunities in Ethiopia and the development of various industries in Ethiopia such as mining and agriculture; the other is to allow Italy to colonize the Agaton province of Ethiopia. (27th, National News Agency Dispatch)

Sovereign Independence What Ethiopia Strives For 30

Addis Ababa According to today's news here, the Ethiopian government has expressed a sincere attitude towards Britain's proposal to mediate the Italian-Ethiopian dispute. According to the Ethiopian King, if Eden's economic proposals to Mussolini do not harm the territorial integrity and sovereign independence of Ethiopia, then Ethiopia is very willing to fulfill them. However, if one wants to open up a corridor for an Italian colony within Ethiopia and establish a police force within Ethiopia, then this is unacceptable to Ethiopia. (27th, National Dispatch)

European Issues Cannot Be Separated 31

(Rome) Regarding the situation of the British-Italian talks, it has now been confirmed that Prime Minister Mussolini insisted that the various issues related to the organization of European peace be mixed together and should not be handled separately. Regarding the Anglo-German naval agreement, the two sides had a thorough discussion on the attitude of Britain in concluding the agreement and its relationship with various European issues, but did not engage in research in technical aspects, largely because Italy did not want to be bound in the slightest. In addition, Italy did not reject or explicitly agree to the dispatch of naval experts to England for talks. As for the Sky Locarno Convention, its establishment will largely depend on whether the European security system can be implemented as a whole. The "Diplomacy" magazine outlined Italy's stance on the Anglo-German naval agreement, saying that "Italy's hesitation is mostly political in nature. If Italy and Germany conclude a naval agreement, stipulating the ratio of naval tonnage between the two countries, how will England deal with it?" The "Fascist Party Work Report" also said that the policy adopted by Britain is not very clear, expressing dissatisfaction. (26th, Havas Dispatch)

(Rome) The Italian newspaper, which is intended to be the mouthpiece of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, made an extremely important revelation today about Eden's visit to Italy, roughly saying that Eden claimed that the Anglo-German naval agreement was only a temporary draft and would only take effect if all the countries concerned agreed to it. Furthermore, the Fascist newspaper also said that the Italian political circles found this explanation by Eden to Mussolini extremely difficult to understand, because if what Eden said was true, then the German side would not be so excited about the establishment of this agreement. The newspaper also said that the foreign policy of Britain is specialized in probing the intentions of others, while adopting a deep and unobtrusive attitude toward its own intentions. (26th, National Dispatch)

British Lords Criticize Anglo-German Agreement - Unilateral Action Allowing Germany to Change the Treaty of Versailles - Saying It Is Enough to Cause a Naval Arms Race Among Countries 32

(London) During the House of Lords meeting today, Conservative Party member Lord Lloyd began debating the naval and military situation influenced by the Anglo-German naval agreement, criticizing the government for changing its policy four times in January, and expressing dissatisfaction with the British government's unilateral action allowing Germany to change the Treaty of Versailles, causing an "atmosphere of disturbance" in France and Italy, saying that Britain now allows Germany to possess a navy equal to 35% of the British navy, while the Washington Naval Treaty limited France and Italy to only 32.5% each. This agreement gives Germany all kinds of conveniences and will trigger a large-scale construction of warships by various countries. Labour Party member Lord Strabolgi followed up by saying that the Labour Party agreed with most of the sentiments expressed by Lord Lloyd just now. If France has concluded an equal submarine fleet agreement with Germany, or if Britain has an agreement with Japan to stab the United States in the back, what will the British government say? Although the Anglo-German agreement is praised for its swiftness in some British circles, he believes that it will eventually prove to be unfavorable. Strabolgi then advocated collective guarantees to protect commercial routes from attack. Liberal Party Marquess of Lothian expressed his opinion that the agreement could increase the hope of achieving a satisfactory result at the Disarmament Conference. Conservative Party Earl Howe did not think so, and said that he intended that the agreement would likely cause a major anti-naval restriction incident. Germany's fleet, having reached 25% of the total number of British ships, will make it impossible for the British fleet to sail east of the Suez Canal in the near future, so the Singapore naval base will lose its effectiveness. Fleet Commander Earl Beatty spoke, saying that he intended that the current British naval strength was insufficient, and the government should urgently invoke the "escalator" clause. He hoped that the current international naval talks could achieve a satisfactory result, so that the Naval Conference could be held this year. As for the Anglo-German naval agreement, judging from the facts of the situation, it is a necessary measure, and the agreement does not hinder other naval countries. If all countries can take the same approach and agree with Germany on land and air armaments, it will greatly benefit Britain and the rest of the world. Before the establishment of the agreement, Britain heard the criticism from France, but the British government could not fail to approve such a treaty that could benefit world peace because of France's opposition. Now, I hope that the French government will understand the overall situation and realize that the agreement will eventually benefit France. (27th, Reuter's Dispatch)

Repercussions of the Anglo-German Agreement - France Increases Defense Spending - Three Drafts Submitted to the Chamber of Deputies 33

(Paris) Three drafts were submitted to the Chamber of Deputies today, all of which were to increase spending in addition to the defense spending set in 1935, including an increase of 1,106,000,000 francs for the army, 1,800,000,000 francs for air defense, and 200,000,000 francs for the navy, totaling approximately £40 million in British gold. This is an echo of the newly established naval agreement between England and Germany. (27th, Reuter's Dispatch)

French Naval Policy - Maintaining Freedom of Action - Will Now Focus Efforts on Building Battleships - Expression of Naval Chief Pietri 34

Brest, France - Navy Minister Pietri recently gave a speech here regarding the Anglo-German naval agreement, roughly saying that Britain's hasty recognition of Germany's naval rearmament was not cautious. The naval figures were something we had almost forgotten, but the ratio of naval tonnage obtained by Germany is enough to make us uneasy. As a result, we will inevitably have to pay attention to naval figures again. From now on, we should concentrate our efforts on the construction of battleships. This is only natural, because the battleships of various countries are restricted by the Washington Naval Treaty, and do not account for a significant tonnage within the total naval tonnage. From now on, we will have the right to free action to make French battleships occupy an important position. (27th, Havas Dispatch)

(Paris) The Senate Naval Committee and Foreign Affairs Committee, which are discussing the Anglo-German naval agreement and French foreign policy, specially extended the meeting time to hear reports from Navy Chief Pietri and Prime Minister Laval. Navy Chief Pietri first stood up to report on France's response to England regarding the Anglo-German naval agreement. Pietri said that since this agreement is a bilateral agreement between England and Germany, France can take complete freedom of action from now on. However, if Britain and other naval countries want to negotiate naval issues with France, they can proceed as usual, without any problems. After Pietri finished his report, Laval stood up to report on the results of his previous tour of Eastern Europe and his talks with Goering in Poland. Laval believes that France's policy must be based on the League of Nations as the main institution for European peace. He mentioned the German note stating that the Franco-Russian mutual assistance agreement does not comply with the Locarno provisions. Laval declared that the conclusion of this agreement was fully approved by the British and Italian governments. Regarding the Austrian issue, Laval declared that if Austria's independence is threatened by foreign forces, France is willing to adopt a cooperative policy with all related countries. Laval continued to say that Hitler's previous peaceful remarks towards France in Congress have opened the door for Franco-German negotiations. If Germany can truly establish coordination with France on the basis of respecting the integrity of all countries, then for the sake of European peace and restoration, I will spare no concessions to accomplish it. (27th, National Dispatch)

German Government Promulgates New Law - Implementing Forced Labor Service - Able-Bodied Men Over 18 Must Perform Compulsory Service - A Six-Month Term as a Preliminary to Military Service - Separate Regulations for Women to Participate 35

(Berlin) The Cabinet passed the Compulsory Labor Service Law at this evening's meeting, stipulating that all young people across the country must perform labor service for six months. In addition, it also passed the Wartime Air Defense Law. Head of State Hitler declared at the Cabinet meeting that the term of compulsory labor service is temporarily set at half a year. In the first year of labor service, all able-bodied men born in 1915 across the country must perform service. (26th, National Dispatch)

(Berlin) The Cabinet passed a decree implementing universal compulsory labor service for men tonight. This is a preliminary to military service. It is heard that the term will be six months. Next year's new "labor army" will be limited to 200,000 people, and will be composed of the 1915 class and volunteers. Volunteers must be at least 18 years old. Women will also join the labor army, but special regulations still need to be formulated, because the female labor corps has not yet reached the capacity to accommodate hundreds of thousands of girls. The new labor army will be named the Labor Service Corps. According to government announcements, this labor service is a matter of honor, so no wages will be paid. (26th, Reuter's Dispatch)

(Berlin) According to the new German law, people over the age of 20 must engage in compulsory labor before serving in the military. This compulsory labor system was recently explained by officials, saying that according to the law, young men and women should engage in compulsory labor equally. However, at present, there are not enough institutions to provide women's labor. If hundreds of thousands of young women across the country joined compulsory labor at the same time, they would not be able to accommodate them. Therefore, the method of women's participation in compulsory labor will be stipulated separately in the future. As for compulsory labor for young men, the Minister of Interior Frick will direct everything, and Colonel Hier will be its leader. According to the Conscription Law, those who are non-Aryan or married to non-Aryans are exempt from military service. However, those of non-Aryan race who are exempted from military service may still participate in compulsory labor, but will not be awarded military ranks. In addition, those who have been deprived of their civil rights due to opposition to the state are exempt from the obligation of compulsory labor. Furthermore, those who reside abroad or wish to go abroad are exempt from the obligation of compulsory labor during their residence abroad. (26th, Havas Dispatch)

Romanian Foreign Minister Rushes to London and Paris - As Representative of the Little Entente - Consultations on the Issue of Middle and Eastern European Pacts 36

(Paris) Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu arrived here this morning and immediately held all-day talks with Prime Minister Laval. The discussion focused on the issue of concluding the Middle and Eastern European Pacts. Titulescu's trip not only represents Romania, but also the Little Entente. Titulescu will also go to London tomorrow to meet with British authorities. (26th, National Dispatch)

French Foreign Minister Receives Russian Ambassador - Discussing International Issues 37

(Paris) Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval received Soviet Ambassador Potemkin in the afternoon to discuss international issues. (26th, Havas Dispatch)

After Naval Funding Is Approved - The United States Begins Building Warships - First Bidding to Add Thirteen Ships - People Within the Navy Department Advocate New Ships to Replace Old Ships 38

(Washington) Secretary of the Navy Swanson announced today that bids for the construction of thirteen warships solicited by the Navy Department will be opened on August 13th. Another eleven ships will also be ordered to be built at naval shipyards after evaluation. Later, Swanson said in a conversation with reporters that the United States does not intend to decide for the time being on the plan to build new ships to replace old ships. It is learned that the government still hopes that the principles of the existing naval treaties can continue to be maintained, so it does not want to implement this construction plan until all hope is exhausted. (26th, National Dispatch)

(Washington) After President Roosevelt approved the $460 million naval funding bill, Navy Secretary Swanson announced today that bidding for the construction of 13 of the 24 warships permitted by the bill will open on August 7th. The Secretary also told reporters that the Navy Department is now studying the number of ships that should be replaced under the Washington Naval Treaty, but no final decision has been made, as it wants to see how other countries act. The opinion of naval department officials has recently changed, advocating replacing old ships with new ships, rather than rebuilding old ships. When reporters asked whether the United States could keep pace with other countries in shipbuilding when the Washington and London Naval Treaties expire, Secretary Swanson replied that the United States does not want to initiate a naval arms race. It is noted that the thirteen ships to be built first are one light cruiser, one aircraft carrier, three destroyers of 850 tons each, five destroyers of 1,500 tons each, and three submarines. (26th, Reuter's Dispatch)

(Washington) Navy Secretary Swanson announced today that the Navy Department has decided to re-implement the naval training centers in Newport, Virginia, and the Great Lakes region, starting on July 1st. These naval training centers had previously been closed under the 1933 austerity plan. (26th, National Dispatch)

United States Plans to Develop South Pacific Aviation 39

(Washington) According to today's news here, in order to develop aviation on the islands of the South Pacific, so as to extend it to Australia and New Zealand in the future, the Department of Commerce will survey the aviation routes in that area. According to the Undersecretary of the Department, the Department's goal is to discover how to make this kind of aviation profitable and safe. (26th, National Dispatch)

Spanish Military Aircraft Formation Flies Around the Country - Journey of Three Thousand Kilometers - Also Performing Aerial Tactics 40

Madrid - Ninety military aircraft, including 30 reconnaissance aircraft, 30 bombers, and 30 pursuit aircraft, departed from the military airfield here today for a three-day flight around the country. This flight is entirely military in nature, and the journey will reach 3,000 kilometers. During the flight, the pilots must practice aerial tactics, and will fly to a certain altitude and speed on a designated flight path. For example, between Madrid and Albacete, they must fly to an altitude of 6,000 meters, at which time the pilots must use oxygen equipment. The pilots have all received detailed secret orders. (27th, National Dispatch)

British and German Approval Sounds, Japan Adjusts its Relationship with Russia, Hirota Proposes Establishing a Border Commission, Russia Protests Over Red Army Shooting Incident 41

(Tokyo) On the afternoon of the 26th, Soviet Russian Ambassador to Japan, Yurenev, visited Foreign Minister Hirota to reiterate a protest regarding the shooting of Soviet Red Army soldiers in early June on the Russian-"Manchukuo" border. Hirota explained the content of reports received from the military, adding that the shooting of Russian soldiers by Japanese troops was an act of legitimate self-defense and that the Russian protest was groundless. The Foreign Minister further stated that if a commission were established to mediate border disputes between Japan, "Manchukuo," and Russia, it could prevent all untoward incidents and quickly resolve matters. The Soviet Russian government has previously agreed in principle to establishing such a commission. He asked if a concrete plan could be proposed soon to achieve this. The Russian ambassador replied that he would seek instructions from his government on this issue. The Foreign Minister continued, saying that the Russian government's current concentration of large forces on the Far Eastern border to strengthen border defenses gave an unpleasant impression to the relations between Japan, "Manchukuo," and Russia. The Russian government should consider withdrawing a portion of its Far Eastern garrison. (27th, Domei News Agency dispatch)

(Tokyo) The proposal for establishing a joint Japan-Soviet-"Manchukuo" commission, agreed upon during the Hirota-Yurenev meeting, is Japan's counterproposal to the Soviet Union's proposed non-aggression treaty. It is reported that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs is currently studying the original plan, which includes the following points: (1) A central committee will be permanently stationed in Harbin, with small committees established in several key border locations such as Manzhouli, Daheihe, and Suifenhe. (2) The small committees will be composed of representatives from the governments of the three countries in the region, including military commissioners. (3) If a small committee cannot resolve a dispute, it will report to the central committee in Harbin. If the central committee cannot resolve the issue, it will be transferred to negotiations between the governments of Japan, the Soviet Union, and "Manchukuo." (27th, Dentsu dispatch)

Northeastern Anti-Japanese Armies Active, Gathering a Thousand People to Attack Tumo Village, Japanese and Puppet Troops Fall into Hard Battles 42

(Harbin) Every year during the time when the green crops grow tall, the anti-Japanese armies are particularly active. This year, coupled with a poor harvest, rural areas are close to famine. Many farmers are joining the anti-Japanese armies, causing their numbers to double, restoring the strength they had soon after September 18th Incident. The North Manchurian anti-Japanese armies are stationed in more than forty locations, appearing and disappearing unpredictably. According to the Iwatsuki unit of the Japanese army stationed in Harbin, between January and May of this year, the anti-Japanese armies fought with the Japanese army seventy-nine times. Furthermore, this year's heavy rainfall has made the fighting particularly difficult for the Japanese army. (27th, China United News Agency dispatch)

(Changchun) According to information received locally today, about a thousand members of the Big Sword Society "bandits" attacked the Right Wing Banner of Tumo Village in Jinzhou Province at 2:00 PM on the 18th. The United States Continues to Purchase Silver, Treasury Department Actions Are Unpredictable, Silver Legislation Temporarily Shelved 49

(Washington) Local authorities indicated today that the recent decline in silver prices is merely a technical adjustment in the global silver market, due to the current supply and demand relationship. It is said that the recent surge in sales of physical silver has overwhelmed the U.S. Treasury Department and other purchasers. However, the primary source of these sales is unknown. (It is generally believed that India is the largest seller. However, it is claimed in Washington that there have been no recent events that triggered the decline. However, the Treasury Department is unwilling to be manipulated by speculators, so all of its actions are designed to thwart speculators. Some believe that the imminent adjournment of Congress, with no new silver legislation being proposed in the near future, may be one cause of the decline. Silver advocates in Congress have encountered political difficulties because rising silver prices are very harmful to China, and U.S. agricultural exports have also declined considerably in the past year. Therefore, the government's silver policy has been heavily criticized. Recently, the Treasury Department's actions have been very secretive, and there is no time limit for achieving the goal of a gold-to-silver ratio of three to one, making it difficult to predict the silver issue. Treasury officials, as they still need to purchase silver, are naturally unwilling to reveal the truth. Although silver advocates in Congress still hope to pass some silver legislation during this session of Congress, President Roosevelt's wealth redistribution plan has become the most important issue in Congress, forcing other matters to be temporarily shelved. (26th, Guomin News Agency dispatch)

Rapid Rise of Jiang and Xiang River Levels: Water Mark Exceeds Last Year's Highest Record; Multiple Critical Dikes and閘s in Wuhan Show Signs of Danger; Supervisory Office Notifies Water Conservancy Agencies to Defend Against Floods 90

Hankou Correspondence: Recent continuous heavy rainfall has caused the Jiang and Xiang Rivers to rise simultaneously. Wuhan, situated at the confluence of these two rivers, experiences a particularly drastic increase in water levels. On the 23rd and 24th, the water rose by 1.2 meters each day, followed by 1.1 meters on the 25th and another 1.2 meters on the 26th. Within a few days, the water level has risen approximately five feet. According to the Jianghan Customs water gauge, the level on the 26th reached 39.2 meters, exceeding last year's highest recorded level and continuing to rise, indicating an increasingly severe situation. In the Wuchang area, some dikes and sluice gates have already shown cracks. In Hankou, the Zhanggong Dike and Jinyin Lake also exhibit precarious conditions. The Fenjin Furnace drainage sluice gate is nearly level with the river surface, all of which require serious attention. The provincial and municipal authorities have separately established flood prevention committees working around the clock with great urgency. The provincial capital, from Qingshan to Jinkou, has been divided into four sections, each with an engineering team of 50 people stationed to repair and defend the dikes. Survey teams have also been dispatched to work. The Hankou Flood Prevention Committee held a meeting today, resolving to establish the first and second flood prevention sections ahead of schedule, each headed by a section chief to oversee operations. The budget will be adjusted according to the water level and submitted to the National Economic Council for approval. Regarding dike patrols, in addition to patrol personnel, the Director of the Jianghan Engineering Bureau and all members of the provincial and municipal flood prevention committees have also been dispatched to inspect their respective sections to ensure thoroughness. The Lianghu Supervisory Commissioner's Office has also dispatched Section Chief An Mengzhou to inspect the dikes. Reports indicate that at Huangwuli on the Wufeng Dike in Wuchang, four cracks have been found in the dike's body, the largest being about two zhang wide and over a foot deep, with a subsidence of more than a foot. The smaller ones are about a zhang long and three or four inches wide. This location is the breach point of the major flood of 1931. The entire dike project is most vulnerable at this point. Supervisory Commissioner Gao Yihan specifically notified all water conservancy agencies on the 26th to pay close attention to prevent breaches. (26th)

Financial Stability in Hankou: Money Shops Organize Adjustment Committee and Public Treasury; Banks Undertake to Release Loans with Large Amounts of Cash Shipped to Hankou 91

Hankou Correspondence: During the final accounting period of 1934, Hankou's financial situation suddenly experienced unprecedented panic, with money shops bearing the brunt. The collapses of Yuanyuan and Zhongyuan were followed by the suspensions of Dayuan, Delong, and Yongmao, causing widespread alarm and anxiety throughout the city. Stabilizing the entire financial system has become the sole objective of the government and the financial sector. The main measures include the establishment of a public treasury by government banks to provide loans to money shops, and the organization of a public treasury by money shops to provide loans to commercial firms, offering assistance at each level and maintaining mutual support. Furthermore, due to a shortage of cash, efforts are being made to ship cash to Hankou for circulation. The Central, China, Communications, Farmers, and Hubei Provincial Banks, responsible for organizing the public treasury, held meetings and decided that, as a first step, each would prepare 200,000 yuan, raising a total of one million yuan in cash to provide loans to money shops, with the Bank of Communications designated as the representative, without setting up a separate agency. On the money shop side, a public treasury is being established, with Xiesheng, Yanyuan, Zhengji, Anyu, Changyu, Gengyu, Ruilong, Chengcheng, Xinshui, Zhengyu, Fuyuan, Junyu, Huihe, and Chengji each contributing 30,000 yuan, and Jinhebao, Yuxinfeng, Lianyi, Lifeng, and Yuanfeng each contributing 20,000 yuan, totaling 540,000 yuan as the public treasury fund. Li Dezhai, Wang Shanchen, Cao Tingxian, Wang Bishuang, Wang Jingyuan, Kang Buyun, Wang Xinfu, Jin Fuqing, Zhao Yuting, Yu Xiaopu, Tang Mingchen, Luo Daohe, Xiao Baoshan, Zeng Yongchen, Zhou Chunzhi, Xu Shengjie, Xiao Heqing, and Xiao Fengzhang have been appointed as committee members, responsible for accepting loans from fellow businesses and foreign firms. A temporary financial adjustment committee has also been established, with Wang Bishuang as the director, responsible for presiding over the committee's affairs and allocating funds. Accountant Wu Jingheng and Cao Yanxian are responsible for accounting matters, while Wang Shancheng and Zhou Chunzhi are responsible for the custody of collateral and funds. Li Dezhai, Sun Kunshan, Wang Xinfu, Kang Buyun, Xiao Heqing, Zhao Yuting, Jin Fuqing, Hui Yongchen, and Xiao Baoshan are responsible for reviewing the quality of collateral goods. Yu Xiaopu, Luo Daohe, Guan Fuju, Xu Shengjie, and Kang Mingchen are responsible for investigating the value of collateral. As for cash, Hankou itself is lacking. On the 25th, the Central, China, and Communications Banks jointly telegraphed their head offices, allocating 2 million yuan in cash, which was shipped to Hankou by boat that day. On the 26th, the Bank of Communications independently obtained approval to ship another 1 million yuan in cash. All of this is expected to arrive within three or four days. Therefore, the financial market has stabilized, and public confidence has greatly increased. In the short term, there should be no further panic. (26th)

Provinces, Cities, and Counties Nationwide Establish Anti-Opium Associations in Compliance with Orders; Headquarters Promulgates Organizational Regulations, Specifying Duties and Aiming for Practical Results 92

Hankou Correspondence: In addition to establishing the Anti-Opium General Association in Wuchang and announcing its organizational regulations, the Headquarters, in accordance with its prescribed measures for implementing opium prohibition, requires all provinces, cities, and counties to separately organize anti-opium committees and sub-committees. It has also formulated the "Organizational Regulations for Anti-Opium Committees and County Sub-Committees in Provinces and Cities," ordering all provinces, cities, and counties to establish them by a set deadline and actively proceed to achieve practical results. The contents of these regulations are detailed below: Article 1: Anti-Opium Committees in provinces and cities and sub-committees in counties shall be organized in accordance with Article 9 of the Implementation Measures for Opium Prohibition by the Headquarters of the Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission. Article 2: A Provincial Anti-Opium Committee shall consist of seven to nine members, while a City Anti-Opium Committee and a County Sub-Committee shall consist of five to seven members, all selected from enthusiastic and impartial individuals in the local community who are committed to opium prohibition. Among the members, three shall be designated as standing committee members to handle daily affairs and execute resolutions. The Headquarters may send personnel to participate in the Provincial and City Anti-Opium Committees, while the Provincial Anti-Opium Committee may send personnel to the County Sub-Committees to supervise and assist in their work. Detailed resumes of all committee members of the Provincial and City Anti-Opium Committees shall be submitted to the Headquarters for record, while resumes of County Sub-Committee members shall be submitted to the Provincial Government for record. Article 3: Provincial and City Anti-Opium Committees and County Sub-Committees shall be established in the locations of the respective Provincial, City, and County governments. Article 4: Local governments shall be responsible for executing all opium prohibition affairs. The committees and sub-committees shall be responsible for supervising, urging, reporting, correcting, designing, investigating, auditing, and advising the opium prohibition agencies. However, the promulgation of opium prohibition announcements shall still be carried out by the Provincial, City, and County governments. Article 5: Provincial and City Anti-Opium Committees shall establish two sections, while County Sub-Committees shall establish two units. The number of personnel in each section or unit shall be determined based on the complexity of the tasks. Article 6: The responsibilities of the Provincial and City Anti-Opium Committees and County Sub-Committees are as follows: Matters related to supervising and assessing the prohibition of planting and smoking; Matters related to assisting in the suppression of smuggling and investigating cases involving opium and drug offenders; Matters related to managing opium addiction treatment centers and planning and allocating their funding; Matters related to reviewing rewards and punishments for personnel involved in the prohibition of planting and smoking; Matters related to auditing all income and expenditure related to opium prohibition and confiscation of drug offenders' assets; Matters related to designing the implementation of prohibition orders and drafting and reviewing propaganda materials and illustrations for the prohibition of planting and smoking; Matters related to drafting opium prohibition documents and reports on resolutions. Article 7: Provincial, City, and County Anti-Opium Committees shall urge local governments to diligently implement all opium prohibition laws and regulations issued by the Headquarters to the best of their ability. Article 8: The Provincial, City, and County soil paste shops and stores, which transport and sell soil paste, shall be managed under the unified control of the Opium Prohibition Inspectorate. Local governments and public security bureaus or local defense forces shall, in accordance with the various opium prohibition regulations of the Headquarters and the regulations on rewarding the investigation and suppression of drugs, consult with the Opium Prohibition Inspectorate to effectively assist in handling private trafficking and sales. Article 9: If officials at all levels responsible for implementing opium prohibition are found to be perfunctory, negligent, or engaging in dereliction of duty or corruption, the committees may correct or report them. Article 10: Provincial and City Anti-Opium Committees and County Sub-Committees shall hold meetings once a week. Emergency meetings may be convened when necessary. Article 11: County Sub-Committees shall prepare reports on opium prohibition work in their respective counties, while Provincial and City Anti-Opium Committees shall compile and print reports on opium prohibition work in their respective provinces and cities. Article 12: All levels of anti-opium committee members shall not receive salaries, but may be reimbursed for travel expenses. Article 13: In addition to hiring essential staff, all levels of anti-opium committees may also assign staff from various levels of government to serve concurrently. Article 14: The budget for the operating expenses of all levels of anti-opium committees shall be approved by the Provincial, City, and County governments and managed under the opium prohibition or allocated revenue items in the respective provinces, cities, and counties, and reported to the Headquarters for record. Article 15: If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, the anti-opium committees at all levels may supplement them in their organizational regulations and detailed rules of procedure, in accordance with the opium prohibition laws and regulations of the Headquarters, and report them for record. Article 16: These regulations shall take effect from the date of promulgation. (25th)

Anhui Provincial Government Plans for Both Flood and Drought, Dispatches Personnel to Inspect River Dikes 93

Anqing Correspondence: The Anhui Provincial Government, noting that rainfall had been scarce since the beginning of summer, leading to an increasing drought, formulated eight emergency measures for drought relief, ordering all counties to comply. It also repeatedly instructed all counties and radio stations to report local weather conditions daily. However, in recent days, all areas have reported rainfall, and the rain has been continuous, causing rivers to rise. As a result, the general public fears the arrival of floods, causing widespread anxiety. The Provincial Government, noting that Tongcheng, Wuwei, Hexian, Fanchang, Wuhu, Dangtu, Susong, Wangjiang, Huaining, Dongzhi, Guichi, and Tongling counties are located along the Yangtze River and heavily rely on irrigation, has realized the critical importance of opening sluices and breaching dikes. Given the potential for hesitation or delayed requests for instructions, which could lead to missed opportunities, the government deemed it necessary to dispatch personnel to conduct inspections as soon as possible. These personnel are to assess the extent of the disaster, observe the river tides, and prepare in advance for the opening of dikes. In areas where the terrain is high and difficult for the river tides to reach, they should assess the terrain and prepare for the installation of water pumps. Furthermore, as the summer flood season has arrived and the floodwaters are increasing daily, it is necessary to ensure the safety of the river dikes while preventing drought. Therefore, the government has copied and distributed dike opening measures to the aforementioned counties, and ordered Wang Deyu, a technician from the Department of Construction, to jointly inspect the river dikes. If there is a need to open sluices or breach dikes, or if the dike situation is precarious, the relevant county government should immediately order the conscription of laborers to carry out emergency repairs to quickly remedy the situation, without delay. They are also instructed to report back for assessment after the event. Furthermore, according to reports, the Huai and Si River areas have a network of rivers and canals, but due to years of neglect, the water conservancy situation is poor. Although Meng and other counties have undertaken river works this year, there has been no overall planning, and many projects have been suspended due to the busy farming season. If these projects are not continued, it is feared that during the flood season, water will flow to low-lying areas, causing the people to suffer from the harm of river dredging. It seems that they should continue to carry out these projects during the slightly less busy farming season. The government has also ordered the counties to continue working on unfinished river projects during the farming slack season to ensure their complete completion. It plans to dispatch personnel to conduct inspections at any time to observe the results. (June 24th)

Songjiang: Administrative Conference Opens 94

The tenth administrative conference of this county, approved by the provincial departments, opened this morning (27th) at 9:00 AM. Wang Zhewu, Standing Committee member of the County Executive Committee, Lu Shulian, Standing Committee member of the Supervisory Committee, and Sun Shiheng, director of the guiding Party committee, all attended. Heads of various county departments and bureaus, district chiefs, and appointed members such as Cai Guangyao all attended on time. County Magistrate Jin Tigan presided over the meeting and observed the formalities. Standing Committee member Wang and Party Committee Director Sun gave speeches. Wu Zhongyu, the secretary, was elected as the vice-chairman, and members of the review committees for public security, finance, construction, education, autonomy, and special groups were appointed. The meeting then adjourned. The first general meeting was held at 1:00 PM in the afternoon, and seven resolutions were discussed and approved. Among the more important ones were the county magistrate's proposal to discuss methods for protecting Huating and Xitang to prevent risks and safeguard the lives and property of the people. It was resolved that the surtax of one cent per mu for land survey fees would be changed to a sea dike support fee, to be stored for the purpose of repairing sea dikes. Other resolutions included reorganizing the streets in the urban and suburban areas, adding garbage bins and public toilets, prohibiting the dumping of garbage, sewage, and dirty water into the city rivers, urging farmers to dredge rivers through compulsory labor, urging the Songjiang Electric Company to quickly sign a power supply contract with the Shanghai Chinese Electric Company to promote morning industries, establishing a reformatory for opium offenders, and adding long-distance telephones to facilitate intelligence, all of which have concrete measures.

Jinshan: Reconstruction of Yangjia Bridge Completed 95

The Yangjia Stone Bridge in Wuben Township, Fourth District, Zhangyan Town, Jinshan County, had a wider river channel and a very narrow bridge surface, making passage extremely difficult during rain and snow. This spring, District Chief Yu and Zhang Qifeng, a local gentleman, raised funds to widen the bridge surface, and the work has now been completed. The villagers are full of praise.

Nanhui: Road Construction on Nanchuan Road Causes Dispute 96

The earthwork construction project for the Chuanzhu section of the Nanchuan Road in the county has been underway for nearly ten days. Yesterday, starting from the Fanjiamaotou section, hundreds of women and children gathered to block the workers, claiming that the road route did not follow the Qintang River and occupied a large amount of farmland. The Second District Chief, Chuan Zhenping, tried to dissuade them without success and urgently reported to the county government. The county government ordered Mou Yizhi, the water patrol team leader of the Public Security Bureau, to lead a team to Zhuzhou overnight to suppress the situation. At the same time, he telegraphed the foreman to strictly follow the regulations when digging ditches and taking soil, and not to exceed them in any way, in order to alleviate the people's difficulties.

Wuxi: Ministry of Finance Sends Personnel to Inspect Stamps 97

The Ministry of Finance, noting that the sales of stamp tax tickets have greatly decreased since they were transferred to local post offices for sale, has specially dispatched Wang Wenwei, a member of the Local Donation and Tax Reform Committee, and "Stamp Inspection Commissioner of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai" to conduct spot checks in various places to clarify the actual sales of stamp tax tickets in various provinces and counties. Commissioner Wang arrived in Jiangsu a few days ago and began conducting spot checks. Yesterday, he arrived in Wuxi and contacted County Magistrate Wang and Xu, the president of the local court, and Yang Hanxi, the chairman of the county chamber of commerce, respectively, and asked for their assistance. It has been decided that, starting today, spot checks will be carried out on various businesses in the urban area. Those who have failed to affix stamps, affixed insufficient stamps, or affixed stamps in an improper manner will be handed over to the respective public security sub-bureaus and then to the county court for fines.

Outbreak of Epidemics in Urban and Rural Areas 98

Since the beginning of summer, the weather has been erratic, with alternating cold and warm spells, leading to the spread of epidemics. A strange disease has recently been discovered in the Xinan Township area of the Third District. Patients experience brain swelling and a blackened face, with trembling limbs, and die within four hours. The mother of Fang Genxiang, a resident of the Huadafangzhuang Jiangzhaowan in the township, suddenly suffered from this disease at around 5:00 AM yesterday and died at around 8:00 AM. Xu Rulei, a resident of Shenjiaqiao, and Hua Ashou, a resident of Longjuezui, have also died from this disease. Furthermore, true cholera and cholera-like epidemics have recently been discovered in the urban area. The information has been reported to the Infectious Disease Inspection Department of the Nanjing Health Department for verification.

Changzhou: Vagrant in Reformatory Tries to Escape by Digging Wall 99

The county government recently appointed Sun Haosheng as the director of the Wuyi Vagrant Reformatory. While he was rectifying everything, on the night of the 25th, Zhao Lagou and Wang Da, vagrants from Qingxiang in the infirmary, colluded to dig a hole in the wall in an attempt to escape. They were spotted by night patrolman Xu Fuyuan, who immediately arrested them. Police Chief Kong Debiao reported the incident to the director, who went to investigate and found a large hole in the wall. When the two vagrants were interrogated, Zhao Lagou confessed that he had secretly hidden a large nail taken from a pillar and used it to dig the wall after being locked up, and that Wang Da had helped him move bricks. Director Sun, considering that the incident was discovered early and did not lead to a major disaster, sent the two vagrants to the county government for interrogation.

Changshu: Large Batch of Opium Traffickers Sent to Province for Investigation 100

The County Anti-Opium Association is currently strictly investigating opium offenders. Recently, it arrested opium traffickers Liu Shaoqing, Peng Xing, Song Xian, Peng Chenshi, Gu Hechang, and Wang Er, as well as heavy opium smoker Feng Chunyuan, totaling seven people. After interrogation and confirmation of the facts, it was approved to send them to the Provincial Anti-Opium Association for review. Today, bailiffs Zhang Chunlin, Liu Yetang, and Qian Zilin were dispatched on the 27th to take a steamer to Zhenjiang and send them to the Garrison Headquarters for interrogation.

Yangzhou: Fire Destroys House and Burns Elderly Woman to Death 101

Yesterday, Jiang Xiaosi, a farmer from Cao'anhou Village, Maqiao River East Township, Fourth District, Jiangdu, had to replant small seedlings due to rain. The whole family went to work in the fields, leaving his mother-in-law, Old Woman Ma, at home to cook. Old Woman Ma, who was nearly seventy years old and frail, accidentally left the fire in the stove next to a pile of firewood. The fire quickly raged, shooting straight through the roof. When Jiang saw it from the fields, he rushed back to save her. All the miscellaneous items in the house were turned to ashes, and Old Woman Ma was burned, her hair and skin damaged. She collapsed in a corner of the wall. Old Woman Ma died from the effects of the fire.

Another Section of the Liuyi Riverbank Collapses 102

Another section of the Liuyi Riverbank, east of the Zhenyang Bus Station, collapsed on the morning of the 26th. It is said that the collapse has actually slowed down the river flow. Initially, the flow coming from the west side would hit the protruding point on the east side, causing a U-turn right at the bus ferry terminal. This created a large whirlpool under the terminal, making the situation increasingly dangerous. Now that this point has collapsed, the return wave has been reduced, which has also reduced the scouring effect of the whirlpool at the terminal entrance. According to employees of the Zhenyang Bus Company, the depth of the water outside the shore is still around one zhang, while the depth within one zhang is about four feet. Therefore, mud and wooden stakes are being placed for reinforcement. If there are no further changes after the mud placement, the ferry can resume docking on the 27th.

Nanjing: Changfeng News Agency Schedules First Publication 103

Niu Yongqing, the son of the late Yan Pisheng, a prominent figure in the Minkang News and a pioneer in the field of commentary, utilizing his family's academic background and taking advantage of his spare time from studying, has joined forces with several like-minded colleagues who possess knowledge of the news industry to organize the Changfeng News Agency, with its headquarters in Dingguanying, Nanjing. It aims to report on all current events with a purely objective style and has scheduled its first publication for July 1st.

Nantong: Two Bureaus Rectify City Appearance in Urban and Suburban Areas 104

The Public Security and Construction Bureaus of Tongyi are currently jointly rectifying the city appearance in the urban and suburban areas, eliminating obstacles to traffic and improving customs. They are also filling in the city rivers that wind around the city and building a slaughterhouse outside the South Gate. Dangerous buildings will be forcibly demolished and repaired.

Violent River Tide Attacks, Causing Bank to Collapse and Break 105

The riverbank in Nantong has been collapsing severely recently. Continuous strong winds and rain have caused the river tide to rise violently, attacking the embankments and causing the riverbank to collapse and break in many places. Farmers have gathered day and night to protect it, but the dangerous situation has not been alleviated. The Construction Bureau has rushed to carry out emergency repair projects.

Jiashan: Second Highway Robbery of Boats Occurs 106

At noon on the 24th, the Gujia boat from Xitang to Pinghu was robbed in front of the Youfang in the south of the East Gate. The case has not yet been solved. The boat of Xu Ahua, from Zhefengjing to Qianyao, was also threatened by two bandits on the afternoon of the 16th near Hezuizi. The two bandits, wearing blue serge long gowns and speaking with a Hunan accent, threatened the boat with box cannons, forcing it to stop. The two bandits jumped down and robbed separately. One passenger, surnamed Zhang, was carrying more than thirty yuan of silver, which he intended to use to buy goods in Qianyao. All of it was robbed. The boat's total loss was no less than one hundred yuan. The boat has reported the incident to the Qianyao Water Police Team, which has dispatched a team to pursue the bandits, but they have already fled far away.

Jiaxing: Kidnapper Re-trial Concludes with Verdict 107

The case of the kidnapping of farmer Feng Abao from Limin Township, Xinfeng, Jiaxing, has resulted in the arrest of Yuan Yigen, Zhao Dayu, Zhang Yimin, Ye Laosan, and four others. After interrogation by the Jiaxing Local Branch Court, Zhao Daxing, Yuan Yigen, and Zhang Yimin were sentenced to death. The verdicts were submitted to the High Court and then to the Provincial Government for review and approval. Zhao and Yuan were executed by shooting in the western suburbs of Jiaxing on June 11. Zhang Yimin was sent back for re-trial. After being re-tried by the criminal court judge on the 20th, the verdict was announced yesterday afternoon. Zhang Yimin's sentence was reduced to fourteen years of imprisonment and will be sent to prison for execution.

Xiaoshan: Children Kidnapped During Nighttime Robbery 108

The home of Cao Weixian, a villager from the Huilangcao area outside the East Gate of Xiaoshan, had some savings, which attracted the attention of bandits. On the afternoon of the 24th, more than ten bandits suddenly arrived, wearing white cloth shirts and pants, wearing felt hats, holding torches, and speaking with a mixed accent. They broke into the house. Cao and others were awakened from their sleep and knew that they were bandits, so they did not dare to speak out and allowed them to rob them. They stole 270 yuan in silver, as well as clothes, quilts, and other items. Then they took away a four-year-old child and fled. The County Public Security Bureau, upon hearing the news, dispatched police officers to the scene of the incident on the 25th to investigate and make arrangements to apprehend the bandits.

International Commercial Telegram - A Special Reuters Commercial Report, June 27 109

Gold and Silver

British Gold: London gold prices continued to rise slightly, today's listing being 141 shillings, 3 and a half pence, up one and a half pence.

British Silver: The London silver market was quiet this morning. Spot price was 31 pence, 0.0625; futures were 31 pence, 0.325. American investment went ahead, with Chinese both buying and selling. Speculators, however, sold. Market conditions were stable at closing.

Exchange Rates

British-American: The London foreign exchange market was very stable this morning. The price of the pound sterling against the dollar and the franc did not change much. The British-American exchange rate opened at $4.94125, the same as yesterday's US-UK closing. Within the first hour, it fell 0.0625 to $4.940625 and remained unchanged until 2 pm.

British-French: Opened at 74 francs 56, up 6 points. Within the first hour, it dropped 2 points to 74 francs 54. This price remained unchanged until 2 pm. Before noon, the British Exchange Equalisation Account sold francs.

Cotton and Wheat

American Cotton: The New York cotton market had nothing particularly exciting. Opening prices were similar to yesterday's closing, with a slight upward trend.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market was slightly firm this morning. At 1 pm, the July contract was 6.35, up 3 points.

British Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market opened steady, but prices eased due to large-scale selling by retail investors and profit-taking on July long positions. Later, prices recovered slightly due to a poor US weather report. At 1 pm, the July contract was 5 shillings, 3 pence, down 0.25.

American Wheat: The Chicago wheat market opened lower, due to improved weather conditions in the producing regions. The same was true for coarse grains.

Rubber

London: The London rubber market was quiet at the opening, then turned sluggish. At noon, the July-September contract was 5 pence 0.9375, up 0.0625.

New York: The New York rubber market opened slightly lower today following news from London, and also because of continued profit-taking on July long positions. After the opening, forward contracts became firmer, returning to yesterday's closing prices.

Securities

New York: The New York stock market opened with fairly strong sentiment. Prices rose slightly across the board. Merchants were quite enthusiastic because President Roosevelt's new tax bill may not pass the House of Representatives in the near future. At the opening, the Dow Jones 30 Industrial Stock Average was 117.95, up 31 points. Later, New York Gas and New Jersey Standard Oil stocks both plummeted, and sentiment weakened considerably. Copper stocks remained stable in price, despite the regulation to cancel the industry code. This is because June 30 is the date for clearing inventories, and producers are unwilling to reduce prices immediately before this date. The details are as follows:

Local News

Postal Savings Bureau Complies with Ministry Order: Prohibiting All Bureaus from Transporting Silver Dollars on Behalf of Others, to Prevent Unscrupulous Merchants from Smuggling Silver 110

The Ministry of Transportation, upon approval of a consultation from the Ministry of Finance, has issued a special order to the Postal Savings and Remittances Bureau, instructing all its local postal bureaus to prohibit the transportation of silver dollars on behalf of others, in order to prevent unscrupulous merchants from smuggling silver. If such transportation is necessary for business reasons, a passport must be obtained from the Ministry before transportation can be carried out. A reporter from the Industrial News Agency learned from the Bureau yesterday that while it may have been possible to transport silver dollars on behalf of customers in the past, such cases have become rare since the Ministry of Finance issued an order prohibiting it. The Bureau, considering this matter to be related to the stability of local finances, has, in order to thoroughly eliminate the practice, complied with the Ministry's order and has instructed all bureaus to comply accordingly.

Minister Kong Returned to Shanghai Yesterday 111

Kong Xiangxi took the express train from Beijing at 5 pm yesterday and arrived in Shanghai at 11:30 pm.

Qin Fen Paid Respects to Soong Yesterday Morning 112

Qin Fen, Secretary-General of the National Economic Council, accompanied by Liu Jingshan, Director of the Northwest Office of the Council, arrived in Shanghai by train from Beijing at 7:15 am yesterday. After disembarking, they went to Qiqi Road to pay respects to Soong Ziwen, a Standing Committee member of the Council, to report on and request instructions regarding Council affairs. After taking their leave, they went to the Council's Shanghai office to handle official business. Qin and Liu will stay in Shanghai for a few days before returning to Beijing.

Gu Mengyu Visited Huang Yesterday 113

Gu Mengyu, Minister of Railways, came to Shanghai a few days ago for medical treatment. He visited Huang Fu, Chairman of the Administrative Yuan's Peiping Political Reorganization Committee, at Qiqi Road at 9:30 am yesterday, and they had a long conversation lasting over an hour before Gu took his leave. Gu has decided to stay in Shanghai for a period of rest as his health has not fully recovered, before returning to Beijing to resume his duties.

Scheduled to Stay in Beijing for at Most One Week

Chen Yi, Chairman of the Fujian Provincial Government, arrived in Shanghai by the Changsha Maru a few days ago. He was quite busy visiting friends and relatives in Shanghai yesterday. Chen, accompanied by his secretary Lu Linchang and adjutant Chen Yuting, took the night train to Beijing at 11 pm last night to report on the political situation in Fujian Province to the central government. Chen is scheduled to stay in Beijing for at most one week. As for whether he will go to Sichuan to pay respects to Chairman Chiang, it has not yet been determined.

Newly Appointed Minister to Belgium, Zhu Hexiang, Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday 115

Attended a Farewell Reception at Aurora University

Zhu Changed His Departure to August

Zhu Hexiang, the newly appointed Minister to Belgium, as the Aurora University Alumni Association was scheduled to hold a grand tea party at 3 pm yesterday to see him off before his departure, Zhu therefore took the Beijing-Shanghai morning express train from Beijing at 8 am yesterday, accompanied by his secretary Zhou Yitong, and arrived in Shanghai at 2:30 pm in the afternoon. It is reported that Zhu was originally scheduled to depart for his post at the beginning of next month, but due to circumstances, his departure has been changed to August 7.

Year-end settlements of Various Banks 116

All Banks Will Be Closed on July 1st and 2nd

According to the Xinsheng News Agency, in order to handle the year-end settlements, all banks have been extending their office hours internally since yesterday, depending on the business of each bank, but externally they still operate according to regulations. As for savings departments and current account balances, interest has been calculated up to June 20th for the first half of the year, and after June 20th it will be for the second half of the year. The calculation of profits and losses has already begun, and it is expected that the settlement will be completed before July 2nd. On July 1st and 2nd, although banks with busy operations will be closed to the public, they will still be working as usual internally to rush to complete the closing of accounts. The collection and remittance between banks and between money shops and banks has been particularly busy these days.

Closed on the 1st and 2nd

The Bankers Association has stipulated that member banks will be closed on July 1st and 2nd for semi-annual settlement, and will resume business as usual on the 3rd. As for Sundays, with the exception of the Ningbo Commercial Bank, China Banking Corporation, Wing Hang Bank, and Tung Hwa Bank, which will remain open in the morning due to different business conditions, all other banks will be closed. Now, China Banking Corporation and Tung Hwa Bank have decided to close all day on Sundays starting from the second half of the year. As for banks that are not members of the association, such as Taiping, Zhengda, Guanghua, Huizhong, Tongyuan, Xinfu, Yadong, Minfu, Daya, Asia, etc., they have jointly announced that they will be closed all day every Sunday starting in July, and will also be closed for two days on July 1st and 2nd as usual.

Surplus of Large and Small Banks

According to Lin Kanghou, Secretary-General of the Bankers Association, whom a reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency met yesterday, the end of June is the year-end settlement period for banks. The Bankers Association has scheduled its eighth annual general meeting of members to be held at 4 pm on the 28th to report on the association's affairs for the first half of the year. As for the year-end settlements of various banks in the first half of the year, although they have not yet been finalized, it is expected that all banks, large and small, will still have surpluses in this period of industrial and commercial recession, but the amounts will vary. However, it is not known whether there are any bad debts and how many. If a bank has many bad debts, it may appear to have a surplus on the surface, but in reality, it is losing money because bad debts are not easily recoverable.

Sharp Increase in Check Clearings

As the end of June settlement period for banks is approaching, the total amount of checks cleared by the bank clearing house increased sharply yesterday, amounting to 33,788,822.07 silver dollars, including 5,866,565.40 silver dollars in cash and 27,922,256.67 silver dollars in remittances, an increase of two-thirds compared to the previous day. The interest rate for public bond loans was 20%, and the discount rate for public bonds was 25%. The interest rate for cash discounts in the money market was 20%, and the highest rate for head money plus water was 70%. The collection and remittance between money shops and banks was also particularly busy due to the settlement.

Minsheng Company's 1 Million Yuan Bonds to be Issued on July 1st 117

Principal and Interest to be Repaid in Eight Years, with an Annual Interest Rate of 10%

Secured by All Existing Ships of the Company

According to the Guowen News Agency, Minsheng Industrial Co., Ltd., in order to develop navigation on the Yangtze River, has, after a resolution by the company's shareholders' meeting, issued 1 million yuan in corporate bonds. Lu Zuofu, the company's general manager, came to Shanghai in person to negotiate with the banking community in Shanghai, and an agreement has been reached. Jin Cheng Bank will underwrite 400,000 yuan, Bank of China will underwrite 200,000 yuan, Bank of Communications and Zhongnan Bank will each underwrite 100,000 yuan, and Shanghai Bank, Juxingcheng Bank, Sichuan Meifeng Bank, and Sichuan-Kang Colonial Development Bank will each underwrite 50,000 yuan. The bonds will be issued at par and repaid in eight years. Only interest will be paid in the first year. From the second year to the seventh year, 7% of the principal will be repaid every six months. In the eighth year, 8% of the principal will be repaid. The bonds are secured by all existing ships of the company (excluding the seven ships of the newly purchased Jiejang Company). The official issuance will take place on July 1st. The announcement of the board of directors is recorded as follows: Notice is hereby given that the company, after a resolution by the shareholders' meeting, will issue corporate bonds. This announcement is made in accordance with Article 180 of the Company Law: (1) Name of the company: Minsheng Industrial Co., Ltd.; (2) Name of the corporate bonds: Minsheng Industrial Co., Ltd. First Corporate Bonds; (3) Total amount of corporate bonds and face value of bonds: 1 million silver dollars, with bonds divided into two types: 10,000 yuan and 1,000 yuan; (4) Interest rate of corporate bonds: 10% per annum; (5) Method and term of repayment: Repaid in eight years. Only interest will be paid in the first year. From the second year to the seventh year, 7% of the principal will be repaid every six months. In the eighth year, 8% of the principal will be repaid, but early repayment is allowed; (6) No corporate bonds have been issued previously; (7) Issued at par; (8) Total amount of the company's share capital: 1 million silver dollars, fully paid up; (9) Total amount of the company's existing assets: Approximately 4.9 million silver dollars; (10) The deadline for raising funds for these corporate bonds is the end of June of the 24th year of the Republic of China. If the funds cannot be raised by the deadline, subscribers may withdraw their subscriptions. This is hereby announced. Board of Directors of Minsheng Industrial Co., Ltd.

Decision Not to Reduce Salaries of Lower-Level Crew Members 118

Passed by the General Assembly of the Shipping Association

The Shanghai Shipping Association had previously, at the request of shipping merchants, resolved to adopt a contractionary policy, whereby the salaries of all crew members above 15 yuan would be paid at 80%. Subsequently, due to a petition from crew members' organizations, it convened a general meeting of all members at its meeting place on Wuma Road at 3 pm yesterday. The attending executive and supervisory committee members included Yu Qiaqing, Yuan Ludeng, Yang Guanbei, Wang Zigang, Yao Shumin, Chen Yisheng, Zhou Zian, Lu Yingen, Ye Chuanfang, and over thirty other members. Yu Qiaqing, the chairman, opened the meeting as usual. First, Yu reported on the petition from the maritime workers' organizations. According to the representatives, crew members with salaries above 15 yuan cannot make a living if their salaries are paid at 80%, and they requested that shipping merchants show consideration. He then solicited the opinions of all members. After that, the discussion began. The group believed that the maritime workers' request was reasonable and should be accepted. It was unanimously passed that the salaries of lower-level crew members should definitely not be reduced. Whether the salaries of higher-level crew members should be reduced should be decided by each company based on its own financial situation. The remaining motions were passed summarily. The meeting adjourned at 4:30 pm.

Planning to Build a Large-Scale Radio Transmitting Station - Internal Announcement of Land Acquisition from the Public - Songjiang County Has Been Instructed to Comply 121

Due to the development of wireless telegraph services, the existing radio transmitting station of the International Telegraph Administration is insufficient. It has selected 300 mu of land near Qianliang Temple in Xinzhuang Township, west of Shanghai, to build a large-scale radio transmitting station. Regarding the acquisition of land from the public, the Administration has received an announcement from the Ministry of Interior. The announcement states: "It has been approved that the Ministry of Transportation's telegram Cai Zi No. 220 of March 2, 24th year of the Republic of China, states: 'It has been found that in the 20th year of the Republic of China, the Shanghai Wireless Telegraph Main Station of the International Telegraph Administration was attached to the Shanghai Middle School in Lujiabang. The foundation is extremely narrow and difficult to develop. The school buildings are also planned to be renovated and have repeatedly urged relocation. It is imperative to find another open area to relocate the new station. After surveying a vacant area near Qianliang Temple on the Shanghai-Minhang-Nanzhe Road, it was found to be very suitable. It is proposed to acquire 300 mu of land according to the Land Expropriation Law. A plan and layout map have been prepared and submitted to your Ministry for review and approval under Tu Zi No. 490. A bulletin No. 38 was attached. Subsequently, the January 28th Incident occurred in Shanghai, and it was temporarily suspended. Now that the Shanghai Radio Station has been merged with the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau, according to the report submitted by the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau, the need to relocate the transmitting station is even more urgent. The number of transmitters to be installed in the future is even greater than before. It is proposed to continue the acquisition of vacant land at Qianliang Temple and expand it to 300 mu. However, the previous announcement has been more than three years old and has lost its validity. Please consult your Ministry to review the previous case, reissue the announcement, and consult the Jiangsu Provincial Government to order the Songjiang County Government to comply.' After examining the request of the Bureau to acquire 300 mu of vacant land at Qianliang Temple, it is indeed necessary, which is consistent with the provisions of Article 2 of the Land Expropriation Law and should be approved. In addition to consulting for review and response, in accordance with the provisions of Article 9 of the same law, the matters that should be announced are listed below for general knowledge. This is hereby announced. The items are: (1) Person in charge of the undertaking: Ministry of Transportation; (2) Type of undertaking: Development of transportation undertakings; (3) Area of the undertaking: Within the 36th Bao and 51st Tu of Xinzhuang Township, Songjiang County, Jiangsu Province (that is, the vacant area near the Qianliang Temple Station on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway, north of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway and south of Changqiao Town), with a total area of 300 mu."

Royal Dutch Mail Steamer Company Launches Trans-Asian-African Ocean Route: A Sea Voyage of Unprecedented Length, Route Determined and Six Ships Assigned 126

Central News Agency reports that the Royal Dutch Mail Steamer Company, to facilitate transportation between Asia and Africa, has decided to launch an unprecedented long-distance route from the sea to South Africa and from Shanghai to East Africa. It has appointed the Java Shipping Company in this port as the general manager. The first mail steamer departing from Shanghai to South Africa is scheduled to sail on July 7. The details are as follows:

A Long Sea Voyage

Recognizing the absence of direct scheduled services between Asia and Africa, the Royal Dutch Shipping Company has initiated these two routes. The sea voyage is of unprecedented length, requiring 150 days for a round trip for each ship. Therefore, only one sailing per month is scheduled. From now on, Asia and Africa can be directly connected, which will greatly boost trade between the two continents.

Route Determined

The routes for both lines have been determined. The South Africa route runs from Shanghai to Cebu, Manila, Saigon, Bangkok, Singapore, Batavia, Mauritius, Lourenco Margues, Durban, East London, Port Elizabeth, Mossel Bay, Cape Town, and then back from Cape Town to Durban, Tamatave, Reunion, Mauritius, Rcdriguez, Batavia, Singapore, Cebu, and Hong Kong. The East Africa route starts from Hong Kong to Bangkok, Singapore, Batavia, Rcdriguez, Mauritius, Reunion, Tamatave, Durban, Beira, Znuzibar, Mombasa, Mahe, Singapore, and Hong Kong, before arriving in Shanghai.

Designated Mail Ships

The shipping company has designated six mail ships for the long voyages of these two routes. The first ship, the Good Hope, with a deadweight of 5,400 tons, is already en route from Hong Kong to East Africa. It is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on July 5 and depart for the South Africa route on July 7. It is expected to return to Hong Kong on September 27. The second ship, the Barents, is scheduled to depart from Shanghai for various South African ports on August 4. The third ship, the Sweeden Hordijk, is scheduled to depart from Shanghai on September 3. The fourth ship, the Loxleven, the fifth ship, the Tasman, and the sixth ship, the Mindegula, are all scheduled to depart on schedule.

Creditor Representatives Hold Emergency Meeting Yesterday

Expressing Support for Resumption Principles
