The creditors Wang Hongzhang, Chen Zhonggao, etc., have organized the Ningbo Industrial Bank Creditors' Association to handle the registration of creditors' rights free of charge. Wu Zhihao, general manager of Ningbo Industrial Bank, sent a letter to the Creditors' Association yesterday, saying: (omitted above) Ningbo Industrial Bank was affected by the sluggish market and suspended collection and payment. I have heard that your Creditors' Association has sent a letter to the special commissioner Luo of the Ministry of Finance to appoint a liquidator to handle the liquidation of the bank's assets and liabilities. This is appropriate and I have no objection. However, the directors and supervisors of Ningbo Bank are trying to maintain it. In order to take care of the rights and interests of your creditors, I sincerely request your association to forward the letter to the special commissioner Luo of the Ministry of Finance and postpone the handling for 14 days. I hope you will approve it.

It was decided that (A) the following points should be replied to Wu Zhihao in a letter: (1) The procedure for requesting from this association is not in compliance; (2) If you are sincere, you can request from the special commissioner of the Ministry of Finance; (3) We agree in principle to the resumption of business; (4) The names and addresses of the directors and supervisors should be disclosed; (5) The letter has no contact address and will be forwarded by Yu Hualong, the lawyer representing the bank; (B) Send a letter to the special commissioner of the Ministry of Finance: (1) Have you heard anything about Wu Zhihao's letter advocating resumption of business? (2) We agree in principle to the resumption of business; (3) Please inform us of the names and addresses of the directors and supervisors of the bank; (C) Confidential; (D) If necessary, post a warning in the newspaper against the directors and supervisors of the bank. Jiangnan Bank Liquidation News 134

Savings Portion Can Be Repaid in Full, Commercial Portion Depends on Account Collection

Jiangnan Bank held a general meeting of shareholders on the 23rd and resolved to liquidate according to law. The liquidation offices in Shanghai and Suzhou have begun to operate, and the debt registration will be completed within one month. According to Accountant Shen, the savings portion is expected to be repaid in full, and the commercial portion depends on the result of account collection. The details are recorded below:

Registration to be Completed Within One Month

Jiangnan Bank declared bankruptcy at the beginning of the month due to poor turnover, and then held a general meeting of shareholders on the 23rd and resolved to liquidate according to law. They hired accountant Shen Jiazhen, Jiang Yiping, and lawyer Dong Chi to work with Commissioner Huang, who was sent by the Ministry of Finance to supervise the liquidation, to check the accounts. The liquidation office was located in the bank and staff have been dispatched to start work. In order to facilitate the creditors of the Suzhou branch and the Tongli and Nanxun offices, accountants Shen Zhaojiu, Dong Chunbiao, and lawyer Jiang Wanping were hired to be responsible in Suzhou. The liquidation office was set up in accountant Shen's office at No. 59 Dashi Tou Xiang. Notices were posted in both places, and registration was limited to one month.

Savings Deposits to be Repaid First

Accountant Shen Jiazhen, who is responsible for the liquidation, said that the bank had repeatedly received orders from the Ministry of Finance to quickly liquidate and sent staff to supervise the process in accordance with banking law. The savings portion should be repaid first. The amount of accounts collected by the bank is about 1.5 million yuan, plus one-fourth of the savings guarantee deposited with the Ministry of Finance. The total amount is enough to repay the savings deposits, which will be repaid first. As for the commercial portion, it depends on the result of the account collection. The number of months for repayment cannot be estimated at this time.

Chamber of Commerce Submits to the Executive Yuan and Other Institutions Requesting Exemption of Special Industrial Provincial Taxes 135

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, in accordance with the resolution of the Sixth General Assembly, submitted a request to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance yesterday, stating that it was a request for matters. The association held the Sixth General Assembly of Members on June 23. According to the proposal of the Dachung Dyeing Factory Co., Ltd., the government should issue a notice to all provinces that all special industrial products exempted from taxes by the Ministry of Finance should also be exempted from provincial taxes. The original proposal stated that domestic industry is in decline, and the trade deficit is increasing. Under the intrusion of foreign forces, emerging industries are even more difficult to survive. Without the government's solid protection, it is not enough to plan for survival. Therefore, the government has regulations for industrial incentives. All emerging industries that have been reviewed by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and meet the requirements may request the Ministry of Finance to approve special tax reductions and exemptions. Its position is equal to that of products that have already paid unified taxes. It should not bear provincial tax obligations. The meaning is very clear, and the principle that one thing should not be taxed twice has long been established in the decree. However, at present, special taxes are often levied due to the special circumstances of a province. The industrial products that the Ministry approves and rewards with tax exemption are treated the same as imported goods, and are forced to pay taxes twice. Although there are cases where tax reductions and exemptions are granted after it has been clarified that it is a tax-exempt national product, it cannot be said that there are none. However, regardless of the reason, complete disapproval is issued, causing merchants to appeal repeatedly and eventually go astray. Such odd situations violate the established system that one thing should not be taxed twice, as well as the original intention of the government to reward and exempt taxes. Therefore, we propose that the government clearly stipulate measures and issue a notice to all provinces that all industrial products that have been rewarded by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and specially exempted from taxes by the Ministry of Finance shall be exempted from provincial taxes in order to reward and develop industry. Is it appropriate? We respectfully await the general assembly to decide. It is learned that the company's man-made pigment, vulcanized element, has been approved by the Ministry of Finance (Jun) to be exempted from transit tariffs within a certain period in accordance with the Industrial Incentive Law. Unexpectedly, the product is transported to various provinces in the country, and there are tax bureaus that levy taxes in the form of disguised likin. Among them, there are also cases where the company has declared the tax exemption and has been approved, but the Gan Province rejects it on the grounds that it is a common case, and the Xiang Taxation Bureau in Wuzhou, Guangxi, is still in dispute. The main purpose of the original proposal is here. In the past, during the era when likin was not abolished, cases of taxing foreign-style goods manufactured according to machinery, after paying taxes in accordance with regulations at the first port, could still be sold throughout the country without being taxed again. Now that likin has been abolished, each province should no longer have so-called production and sales taxes and other similar names. According to Articles 62, Fifth and Sixth of the Provisional Constitution during the Period of Political Tutelage, and the National Financial Conference of the previous year, the original plan was to abolish exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous taxes. This taxation is originally illegal. Moreover, the central government specially approves the exemption of transit tariffs for items that are subject to the Industrial Incentive Law, but each province still maintains its established situation and insists on taxing them. Not only is the order to abolish likin equal to a mere formality, but also the Industrial Incentive Law is only implemented in the central government, not in each province, which inevitably violates the spirit of unified laws and regulations. It has been resolved by the general assembly to submit to the government for correction and prevention. It is reasonable to record the case and prepare a document to submit to your court (department) for review and approval for implementation.

The济生会 Reports on the Tragic Famine in Liyang 138

Report by Investigator Yin Shunzhang

The Central China Relief Society, in conjunction with various provincial drought relief associations, the Chinese and Foreign Relief Society, and the Liyang Drought Relief Association, is managing spring relief efforts in Liyang. Director Li Yundoujun is in charge of investigation and distribution, with over ten relief workers. The work is nearing completion. Now, investigator Yin Shunzhang has returned to Shanghai and submitted a report on the tragic situation in Liyang, as follows: (1) The sixth and third districts are the most severely affected areas. Famine victims are displaced and have no food, filling their stomachs with white clay and elm bark. In the places surveyed, the elm trees have been completely stripped of their bark. Larger shops in the villages, such as those selling dried goods, Beijing and Guangzhou products, cotton cloth, and sugar, have all closed down. Only a few small stalls, such as pancake shops, tofu shops, and general goods stalls, barely manage to survive. (2) Throughout the villages, famine victims are selling their sons and daughters everywhere. According to surveys, a large number of men and women have been sold in the past year, comparable to the tragic famine in Shaanxi Province in the past. (3) This year, it has not rained for a long time, and farmers cannot plant rice seedlings. The rivers are shallow and dry, and farmers have no money to pump water, so they can only resign themselves to fate. The most miserable account for nearly five-tenths of the population. Since there are no rice seedlings to plant, even with local efforts to find solutions, they have exhausted all resources and can do nothing. Fortunately, this time, there has been timely rain, and the rice seedlings that have been planted can recover. However, the mountain fields cannot be salvaged. (3) Liyang is originally a silk-producing area. In recent years, due to the low price of silk, local silkworm cocoons are worth only eleven or twelve yuan, and improved varieties are worth eighteen or nineteen yuan. Villagers work hard for a spring but do not get their money's worth. No one even cares about mulberry leaves. Many shops in the area have closed down, and the number of unemployed people is increasing everywhere. They have no way to borrow money and no way to beg for food. Many have committed suicide. The hardship is hard to describe in words. The association provides relief as much as possible, but there is not enough to go around. It is difficult to manage the aftermath, and famine victims are dying everywhere. Unable to afford coffins, the association also arranges for this. The association has been running disaster relief in various provinces for many years with great success. In recent years, due to commercial depression and people's suffering, donations have been affected, and the source of funds has been decreasing day by day. This time, when running the Liyang relief effort, with the cooperation of charities, they appealed everywhere and raised a small amount of money to distribute, but it is truly a drop in the bucket. However, they hope that the rain will be abundant in the future, and there will be a good harvest in the autumn, so that the people can recover from their hardships. This would be fortunate not only for Liyang County.

Chen Beisan, the chief prosecutor of the Second Special District Local Court, has been in office for nearly four years since the establishment of the court on August 1, 1931. It is said that Chen, the former chief, has ordered his staff to rush the handover, and the new chief is expected to take office on the first day of next month.

Female Corpse Discovered in a Pile of Gravel 140

Knife wound on the neck

Victim appears to have been dead for several days

In an open space at the corner of Xujiahui Road and Route Ratard in the French Concession, inside a pile of gravel used by the French Public Works Department for road construction, at 11:45 yesterday morning, a laborer digging gravel discovered the corpse of an unidentified woman who had been murdered. The upper and lower body were naked, without a thread of clothing, with cropped hair and unbound feet. The victim appears to have been dead for several days. There was a knife wound on her neck, the cut was very deep. The skin and flesh of her hands and feet had rotted and fallen off, making it impossible to recognize her face. She was approximately thirty years old, and the stench was unbearable. The workers were horrified and immediately informed Officer No. 513 at the nearby Baojian Road Fuxu Police Station. The police chief immediately dispatched Chinese and foreign detectives to investigate. After inspecting the scene, they notified the Tongren Fuyuan Sub-station and ordered workers to transport the body to the morgue, pending an inspection by personnel from the Second Special Court Prosecutor's Office today. In the meantime, the head of the French police detective team has instructed all detectives to strictly investigate the case and bring the perpetrators to justice for interrogation.

Collision Between Chunhua and Qingning on the Huangpu River 141

Inspecting the extent of damage

Preparing for import and repair

The Qingning steamer of the Shanghai-Ningbo Steamship Company was berthed at buoys No. 8 and No. 9 in the Huangpu River, while the Chunhua steamer of the Xinghua Steamship Company was moving from buoy No. 24 to buoys No. 9 and No. 10 at 7:34 a.m. on the 26th. At that time, the tide was rapid, and the hull was subjected to the pressure of the tide, causing it to collide with the Qingning steamer. The Chunhua steamer attempted to retreat to avoid the collision, but it was too late, resulting in a violent impact on the stern of the Qingning, causing damage.

Extent of damage

The Qingning was struck a total of two times. After inspection, the damaged iron plates were found to be uneven for a length of more than six feet, and the dent was more than half a foot deep. The extent of the damage to the internal structure below the stern can only be determined after inspection. The Shanghai-Ningbo Company has, based on the report of the captain of the Qingning, sent a letter to the Xinghua Company requesting that they also send personnel to inspect the damage, and has reported the matter to the Maritime Affairs Bureau for their attention.

Request for inspection

The owner of the Chunhua steamer also reported, stating that when the ship was changing berths from buoy No. 24 to buoys No. 9 and No. 10, the ships were close to each other, and due to the rapid tide, it was impossible to prevent the collision, resulting in slight damage to the iron plates on the stern of the Qingning steamer, causing them to be uneven. They have now received a letter from the Shanghai-Ningbo Company requesting that personnel be sent to inspect and repair the damage. They are now reporting to the insurance company, requesting them to promptly dispatch a marine surveyor to the Qingning to inspect the vessel and determine how it should be repaired, which will be negotiated by the insurance company.

Public Works Bureau to Improve City Traffic 143

Surveying parking lots and installing traffic lights

The Public Works Bureau has determined that the increasing number of vehicles in the city has made traffic more complex, with many major intersections experiencing disorder. They are now working to improve traffic, re-surveying rickshaw parking lots and installing traffic lights at key intersections to improve traffic order and convenience for citizens. The details of the improvement plan are as follows:

Re-surveying parking lots

Traffic has recently become increasingly congested in areas like the Old West Gate and Sishan Road in Shanghai South and Zhabei. Many rickshaws waiting for customers wander into the road, and even compete for passengers, which is not conducive to traffic. It is urgent to designate parking areas to improve this situation. The Public Works Bureau, together with the Public Security Bureau and the Engineering Bureau, sent personnel to Shanghai South and Zhabei on the 6th of this month to conduct on-site surveys. They decided to set up 23 parking areas in the Shanghai South district and 17 in the Zhabei district. All traffic signs have been discussed by the Public Works Bureau and the Engineering Bureau for installation, and it is expected that they will be completed in the near future.

Installing traffic lights

There are still too few traffic lights installed at various intersections in the city. The Public Works Bureau has previously planned to install traffic lights at two locations, the Old West Gate and the Baoshan Road intersection, and handed them over to the Public Security Bureau for management. Since being put into use, the results have been good. Other important intersections, such as the Qimei Road-Songhu Road intersection, the Datong Road-Xinmin Road intersection, the Xieqiao-Zhaozhou Road intersection, the Fangxie Road intersection, the Dongmen Road-Waima Road intersection, the Xiaodongmen-Zhongza Road intersection, the Shangwen Road-Zhonghua Road intersection, and the Waima Road-Dadamatou intersection, have also been surveyed by the Public Works Bureau together with relevant bureaus as locations for traffic light installation. The bureau has now hired workers to install red and green lights, build elevated and ground-level traffic control platforms, and plan no-stopping lines and vehicle stopping lines. All of the above projects are said to have started and are expected to be completed within a month.

Sixty-year-old Man Seduces and Defiles Female Student 144

After living together, he abandons her. Female student sues him.

Luo Zeyu, the elder brother of Luo Zemou, is sixty-one years old. He lives at No. 11, Gudong Road, Dongjie, Fuzhou. He has been doing business in Shanghai for many years, residing at No. 71, Xihu Lane, Ximen Road, French Concession. He opened Henghe Money Exchange in Nanshi, Chinese territory, and has a considerable position in the local community, with substantial assets. Although Luo is over sixty years old, his lust has not diminished. Ye Liangzhen, a woman from the same village, is twenty-nine years old. After graduating from a women's middle school in Hangzhou, she came to Shanghai for further education. In June of the 21st year of the Republic, she was introduced to Luo by a Miss Qiu, who falsely claimed that he had no wife and wished to marry Ye. Ye did not hastily agree, and began friendly interactions. She was then lured into a room at the Far Eastern Hotel and sexually assaulted. Luo then proposed that they rent a house to live together, and then formally hold a wedding ceremony. They rented places at Sanxingli, Beile Road and Nanwenderli, Tianxiangli, and lived together. After some time, Ye discovered that Luo's official wife was still alive. She confronted him and urged him to hold a wedding ceremony. After repeated pleading from Luo, he wrote a permanent support agreement on February 6 of the previous year, and gave it to Ye as proof. From then on, Luo took Ye home to meet his wife, and both addressed each other as sisters, but Luo’s wife did not like Ye and wished for her to leave. Luo abandoned Ye in the Dongfang Apartment. Only after mediation by relatives and friends did Luo rent a place for her at No. 22, Haixue Lane, Chengyuan Road. However, Luo again had his friends provide for Ye's expenses. Later, Luo moved Ye to Wuling Apartment on Balang Road. On December 28 of last year, Luo finally abandoned Ye. After repeated attempts to communicate with him, Luo refused to meet, and no resolution was reached. Recently, Ye, feeling that Luo intended to treat her as a toy, could no longer bear it. She hired a lawyer to file a complaint with the Criminal Division of the Second Special Court, accusing Luo Zeyu of violating Article 244, Section 1 of the Criminal Code, by falsely claiming to be in a marital relationship, engaging in illicit sexual relations, and harming public morals, and also violating Article 309, Section 1 of the same code, by abandoning her. She requested that he be prosecuted according to law, and sought incidental civil damages of 10,000 yuan for mental distress, and 50 yuan per month until the age of 60, as stipulated in the support agreement, totaling 19,200 yuan. Upon receiving the complaint, the court, presided over by Wang Gangxu, Chief of the Criminal Division, opened the Second Criminal Court yesterday afternoon to hear the case. The defendant did not appear. Only the plaintiff, Ye Liangzhen, and her lawyer were present. She described her seduction, cohabitation, and abandonment. The judge ordered the court police to deliver a summons to the defendant. According to reports, the defendant was not present, and had gone to the countryside, or that no such person lived there. According to the plaintiff, the defendant did indeed live at No. 71, Xihu Lane, and she had recently encountered him there. The judge ruled that Luo was deliberately evading the summons, and the hearing was adjourned to July 5, at which time the plaintiff was instructed to bring the defendant to court for further questioning.

Workers Seek Revenge, Wielding Knives in a Frenzy 145

Men injured and lying in pools of blood; three assailants detained

Cao Zhenquan, a worker in the workshop of the Xiangyin Factory in Lujiazui, Pudong, had a feud with Chen Miaoxian, Cai Heshang, and other workers in the same factory. Although friends on both sides had tried to mediate, a satisfactory resolution was never reached. At 5 p.m. the day before yesterday, the factory closed as usual, and over three thousand workers filed out. However, some workers did not leave the factory and lingered around, as if waiting for something. This was noticed by Liu Nuxiu, the factory's petition police chief, who became suspicious and went forward to inquire, urging the workers to leave the factory quickly. Unexpectedly, a tragedy occurred in an instant. Two workers, Cao Zhenquan and Li Jingyi, held foot-long knives and slashed wildly in search of revenge. Police Chief Liu saw this and was shocked. She immediately blew her whistle, calling gatekeeper Zhu Jiaoyao and off-duty policemen Wang Wende and Yao Fusheng to the scene to suppress the situation and stop the attack. However, it was too late. Moreover, there were too many people, making it difficult to manage. Police Chief Liu and the others managed to detain three criminals, Cao Zhenquan, Li Jingyi, and Ren Maoshan. The victims, Cai Heshang, had his arm broken and was slashed in the face, Chen Afu had a knife wound on his neck, and Wang Genrong had a slash wound on the back of his hand. All were lying in pools of blood. Police Chief Liu immediately escorted the criminals to the Pudong Branch Bureau, along with the two knives, and sent them to the local court for questioning and detention. The injured were sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment. Chen Miaoxian, seeing the situation was unfavorable, had fled beforehand and was not injured. Yesterday afternoon, Prosecutor Li Caigui ordered Police Chief Liu Wenxiu and policemen Zhu Jiafan, Wang Wende, and Yao Fusheng to appear in court, along with the detained Cao Zhenquan, Li Jingyi, and Ren Maoshan for questioning. Police Chief Liu and the others described the events and the circumstances of the arrest. As a result, the judge ordered the three defendants to be detained pending further instructions.

Demolition of the Former Bank of China Site 147

Construction of an Eight-Story Building

The former site of the Bank of China at the intersection of Renji Road on the Bund has been actively undergoing demolition since the bank decided to relocate and rebuild. However, the project was delayed for three or four months due to the use of the building for the Shanghai pre-exhibition of the London International Exhibition of Chinese Art, from preparation to conclusion. Only recently did the Xinrenji Construction Company begin demolition. Over a hundred workers are currently employed, working hard to complete the project within three months, at an estimated cost of three to four thousand yuan. The original building's assets were also won by the company, for over 40,000 yuan. The site includes approximately ten mu of land between Renji Road, Yuanmingyuan Road, and Beijing Road on the Bund. According to the Bank of China's original plan, the entire site was to be rebuilt into a 30-story building. However, due to current market conditions, the new building will be approximately eight stories, with a maximum of ten stories. The foundation will still be suitable for a 30-story building, so that additional floors can be added if necessary in the future. The blueprints for the building are reportedly still undecided, and the pile driving process will take two years.

Public Concession Fire Report for May 148

According to the Public Works Department Fire Department's report for May, the department received a total of 106 alarms that month, nine of which were false alarms. The property at risk from the fires was valued at approximately 14,330,000 yuan within the Public Concession and approximately 220,000 yuan within the Special Tax District. Actual losses amounted to over 71,000 yuan within the Concession and approximately 350 yuan in Special Tax District C. The Emergency East Division received a total of 479 emergency calls that month, and a total of 480 injured people were sent to various hospitals. Furthermore, the Fire Department ambulance rescued 17 people who had fainted on the street during the past month. According to the diagnosis reports from various hospitals, the cause was starvation. The total number of starvation cases for the first five months of this year is 54. Furthermore, in May, 42 people who committed suicide or attempted suicide were sent to various hospitals. The number of suicide cases transported to various hospitals by ambulance in the first five months of this year is 127. In addition, there were 49 opium addicts. These cases are not included in the suicide or attempted suicide statistics, but all were poisoned by ingesting opium, which is similar to attempted suicide.

Public Works Department Hospitals: Summary of May Work 149

The Public Works Department Isolation Hospital admitted 23 patients, and its work was relatively light. The number of cases of pulmonary tuberculosis has been increasing, and it is almost impossible to accommodate those suffering from severe lung diseases. Therefore, they have had to release a few patients with milder conditions who have been in the hospital for a long time. The Chinese Isolation Hospital was busier, admitting 94 patients, including 39 with tonsillitis, 15 with scarlet fever, and 2 with rabies. The rabies patients had been bitten by dogs outside the Concession and died in the hospital before they could be treated. The Public Works Department Patrol Hospital admitted 190 patients in May, but its work was not strained. Only one person underwent major surgery. The Indian Patrol Hospital admitted 58 patients in May, and there was nothing special to report. The Ward Road Prison Hospital admitted a total of 118 patients and 19 died, with cases of pulmonary tuberculosis accounting for 14 of the deaths.

Public Works Bureau Organizes Ferry Services 150

In order to organize ferry services on the Huangpu River, the Public Works Bureau issued a notice in July 1934, instructing all ferry operators to submit all ferry boats for inspection. Those that were dilapidated were to be strictly eliminated or extensively repaired, and iron railings were to be installed on both sides of the boat cabins. The ferry operators complied accordingly and reported to the bureau for inspection. A total of 12 ferry docks were inspected, and 100 ferry boats were qualified. The bureau has now determined the number of passengers that each boat can carry according to its capacity, and has manufactured and issued limit signs, which are nailed to the boat in a visible location, strictly prohibiting overloading in order to ensure safety.

The National Christian Council Supports Rural Revival Projects 153

The decline of rural areas in our country in recent years has created various social problems, with huge implications for the future of the nation. The National Christian Council of China has long been concerned about this issue. Three years ago, it allocated a large sum of money and entrusted the Department of Agriculture and Forestry of Nanjing Jinling University to use it for rural revival projects. The university understood this intention well and earnestly carried out the work after being entrusted, achieving remarkable results. The council was deeply satisfied. Zhen Xin Stone Powder Factory Accuses Gu Tian Sheng Factory Owner of Breach of Contract 158

Xue Yongji Severely Beaten, Public Prosecution Already Filed

Xin Sheng Society reports that the various Fei Hua [Flying Flower] factories in the city were previously troubled by the high prices of stone powder, which affected their costs. Therefore, they invited Gu Yongfu, the owner of Gu Tian Sheng Flower Factory, and leaders of the Fei Hua industry, Xie Zhongle and Bao Guoliang, to discuss with Wang Yansong, Luo Qinghua, Jin Jianxiang, Zheng Chengqing, and other prominent figures in the business community to jointly invest in the establishment of Zhen Xin Machinery Stone Powder Factory. Mr. Wang agreed to initiate the organization, as the industry had foreign trade relations. Furthermore, each factory in the industry signed a sales contract to demonstrate good faith. The contract stipulated that they could not purchase stone powder from other factories or companies within five years. If they purchased stone powder from other factories or companies, regardless of the quantity, it would be considered a breach of contract, and they would be liable for damages of 30,000 yuan. However, after Zhen Xin Factory started producing powder, the stone powder factories jointly lowered prices below cost to counteract it. Consequently, Gu Tian Sheng Flower Factory disregarded its credit and secretly violated the sales contract, repeatedly issuing bounced checks for the payment due to Zhen Xin, amounting to a significant sum. Recently, the factory purchased a large quantity of stone powder from another company, which was spotted by Su Yongqing, an employee of Zhen Xin Factory. When he politely inquired, Gu Yongfu, the owner of Gu Tian Sheng Factory, fearing exposure and the need to pay substantial liquidated damages, became enraged. He ordered his son, Gu Yixiang, and boatman Zhao Changqing, along with several workers, to assault Xue Yongqing, causing severe internal injuries. The water patrol team arrested the perpetrators and sent them to the local court for investigation. The injured party was sent to the hospital for treatment, but his condition was critical. The court dispatched personnel to verify the injuries. On the 24th of this month, prosecutor Lei Binzhang opened the court for investigation, leading to the detention of the defendants. Public prosecution was initiated in accordance with Article 293, Paragraph 1 of the criminal law. Regarding the bounced checks and the full amount of the contract breach, Zhen Xin Factory has also filed a lawsuit according to the law.

Seduction of a Minor Case Transferred to Local Court 159

Jiang Maolang from Chongming, residing at No. 442, Yulin Road, Lane 4, sells vegetables. His daughter, Xiaoqing, is seventeen years old. In December of last year, she was seduced by Cao Yilang, a twenty-eight-year-old man from Haimen who cohabitated with her while selling bao fan [steamed buns]. They engaged in sexual relations, leading to a secret pregnancy and a bulging abdomen. Fearing her father's rebuke, Cao, on the ninth of this month, sought help from friends Yang Xuefan, Lao Liming, from Tongzhou, and Cai Rongzhang to find an elderly woman surnamed Mou to perform an abortion. After the abortion, she became ill and was sent to Shengxin Hospital for treatment. On the 24th, she recovered and was discharged. Liu Zhisheng, a detective from Yulin Road Police Station, uncovered the truth and arrested Cao. He also learned about Yang and Ding, who resided at No. 292, Taopeng Road, and subsequently apprehended them. Cai Rongzhang and the abortionist elderly woman fled upon hearing the news. The next morning, along with Jiang's daughter, they were all sent to the Simple Trial Division of the First Special District Court. As the case should be heard by the local court, it was transferred to the Third Criminal Court yesterday morning. Wang Yaotang, a lawyer from the Public Works Department, stated that in addition to the crime of abortion under Article 304 of the Criminal Law, there was also a charge of obscenity and seduction, which had not been added. He requested a postponement. Jiang's daughter had not fully recovered, and her father was present in court, requesting temporary custody pending further investigation. Judge Jiang Shuzi approved this, ordering the three defendants Cao Yilang et al. to be remanded in custody for further review.

Thief Who Snatched Gold Earrings Sentenced to Three Months 160

Old woman Gu Sunshi from Qingpu was walking near the corner of Kunming Road and North Sichuan Road at approximately 3:00 PM on the 19th of this month when Li Asan from Ningbo ran up from behind and forcibly snatched her gold earrings, worth eight yuan. Her ear was torn and bleeding. She cried out in pain, shouting "Robber!" A Westerner nearby saw this and gave chase. At the entrance of Dexing Lane on Peng Road, Li was apprehended. Li seized the opportunity to discard the stolen goods on the ground, which the Westerner recovered. While the Westerner was grappling with Li, Fang Cheng, a Cantonese detective from the Hongkou Police Station, arrived upon hearing the alarm. After learning the details, he took Li Asan and the stolen goods to the police station and then transferred them to the First Special District Court. The defendant denied the charges, claiming that he was startled by the shouts of "Catch the thief" and ran away, and that the gold earrings were taken by someone else. The judge ordered him to be held in custody, and the evidence was returned to Ms. Gu. Yesterday morning, Judge Jiang Shuzi resumed the hearing in the Third Criminal Court. Wang Yaotang, a lawyer from the Public Works Department, stated that the investigation confirmed that the defendant had robbed Ms. Gu's gold earrings. He requested a severe punishment. The defendant continued to offer evasive testimony. Judge Jiang sentenced Li Asan to three months of imprisonment as a warning.

Economic Hardship Leads to Xu Xichang's Suicide by Poison 161

Collapses and Dies Outside the Court

Xu Xichang from Anhui, aged twenty-three, resided in his hometown. A month ago, he traveled to Shanghai but was unable to find work and faced extreme financial difficulties. As a stranger in a new place, he had no one to turn to for help. Overwhelmed by his circumstances, he became resentful and decided to end his life. He secretly ingested opium along the way. However, upon reaching the various Chayang Lane sections of Keneng Hai Road, the poison took effect, and he collapsed and moaned. Hua Bu No. 3177, a patrol officer from the Hui Si Police Station, spotted him and sent him to Tongren Hospital. After some treatment, he was discharged and taken back to the police station. As he had no residence in Shanghai, he was held overnight. The next morning, the police chief ordered him to be sent to the First Special District Local Court for disposition. He was ordered to be sent to the Anhui Fellow Villagers Association. However, after leaving the court and reaching the entrance, Xu collapsed again. Gao Yuqing, a detective passing by, sent him to Tongren Hospital again, but he died before receiving treatment. The body was transported to the Yielun Road morgue. Yesterday morning, the First Special Court appointed Prosecutor Tang to conduct an examination, confirming that the body was male. It was determined that Xu Xichang died from opium poisoning. As there were no known relatives, the body was handed over to the Pushan Villa for burial. The deceased's belongings were sent to the police station for public notice.

Private Car License Renewal Deadline 162

The license for private cars for the first half of this year expires on June 30th. Those who wish to continue to obtain a license for the second half of the year should bring their license and fee to the Public Works Department Donation Office at No. 209, Jiangxi Road, to pay and obtain the new license. Notice for Continuing License Renewal for Chartered Cars 163

Those who wish to continue to obtain an autumn license for privately chartered cars should go to the chartered car license office at No. 596, Gongping Road, to obtain it before July 21st. Those who apply after the deadline will be issued a new license plate and will be charged a registration fee of five jiao in addition to the regular license fee. The license application form is issued by the Public Works Department and can be obtained from the chartered car license office on Gongping Road, or from the Public Works Department Donation Office, and nearby police stations. After filling it out, submit it along with the license fee of eight yuan to the license office. To avoid delays, applicants should ensure that all information filled out on the form is accurate and that all seals and signatures match those on the previous season's application form.

The office hours for the license office on Gongping Road are from 8:30 AM to 12:00 PM and 2:00 PM to 3:30 PM every morning. On Saturdays, the office is open in the morning but closes early at 11:30 AM.

Song Xueqin, Divorced Concubine, Sues for Daughter's Identity 164

Requests Confirmation That Lizhen is Song's Daughter

Song Xueqin, a fifty-seven-year-old man from Wuxing, Zhejiang, was the director of the Shanghai office of Sun Chuanfang, the former commander of the Five Provinces Allied Forces. He followed Sun for many years and was highly regarded by him. He was once prominent, but after the failure, Song also abandoned his political career and became a recluse in Shanghai. He has two residences in Shanghai: one at No. 1, Lane 35, Maite Hesituo Road, and the other at Fushou Lane, Weihaiwei Road. In 1921, Song married Bo Xuezhen (now thirty-four years old) from Wuxian as a concubine, and she gave birth to a daughter named Lizhen, who is now eleven years old. Song and Bo lived together until May 20, 1931, when they divorced due to disagreements. An agreement was made that Song would pay Bo 20,000 yuan and that Lizhen would be raised by Bo. Since the separation, Bo has lived with her daughter at No. 6, Jinle Lane, Weihaiwei Road. However, without legal recognition of Lizhen's identity, her future status and treatment may be affected. Therefore, in accordance with Article 1065 of the Civil Code, which states that a child born out of wedlock is considered legitimate if acknowledged by the father, and that a child raised by the father is considered acknowledged, she has requested mediation from the Mediation Office of the First Special District Court to confirm that Lizhen is Song Xueqin's biological daughter. After the court summoned the parties for mediation without success, Bo formally filed a lawsuit through lawyers Zhang Shizhao, Xiang Xun, and Peng Yuanxun. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, Judge Peng Shi of the First Special Court opened the Fourteenth Civil Court for hearing. Song Xueqin was absent, but his lawyer was present, stating that he had insufficient time to respond and requesting a postponement. After the plaintiff's lawyer stated the purpose of the lawsuit, the defendant's request was granted, and the hearing was rescheduled for July 13th.

Gangster Serving Five-Year Sentence Sent to Court for Review 165

Yan Rulin, a wealthy merchant residing in Changxing Lane on Jielu Road, was building a new house at No. 1325, Lafayette Road, in the French Concession in the spring of 1930. On March 23rd, Yan went to inspect the construction of the new house. However, a group of kidnappers, disguised as carpenters and painters, were working inside. When Yan entered the house, the kidnappers rushed forward and kidnapped Yan, hiding him in a foreign house at No. 356, Jin Shenfu Road. They demanded a large ransom. After being held for a month, the French police discovered and broke up the kidnapping ring, rescued the hostage, and arrested eight kidnappers, including Zhang Fengxiang, Wang Xiaogen, Chen Liangen, Tao Jinbao, and Fang You. After interrogation by the French Public Concession, Zhang was handed over to the headquarters for execution, while the remaining criminals were sentenced to five years in prison and then transferred to the inland government for further investigation. Now, the five-year sentences of Chen, Tao, and Fang have expired. The Second Special District Prison has transferred them to the Second Special District Court for review. Yesterday, Court President Wang Gangxu of the Second Special Court opened the court for interrogation and appointed lawyer Yu Zhongluo to defend the three defendants. Lawyer Gu Shouxi from the Police Department appeared in court to present the case. Detective Zhou Buguang reported the details of the case at that time. The three defendants all denied participating in the kidnapping. After hearing the testimony, the court ordered a debate and then adjourned the case, scheduling the pronouncement of the verdict for the 29th. The defendants remain in custody.

The following is a summary of the society's relief efforts in Jiangxi Province: Since departing for the disaster area in Jiangxi Province in December of last year, the team has been working for six months. Trademark Bureau Publishes 100th Issue Commemorative Issue 181

The Trademark Bureau of the Ministry of Industry was reorganized and established from the National Registration Bureau directly under the National Government in the winter of 1928. It has been seven years since then. The Trademark Gazette, published monthly by the bureau, has reached its 100th issue in June of this year. He Zhuoxian, the director of the bureau, has printed a commemorative special issue of the 100th issue of the Trademark Gazette, which was published yesterday. The content is rich, with inscriptions and prefaces by Chairman Lin, President Wang, Vice President Kong, Minister Chen, Liu, and Gu, and two deputy ministers. He also published an article entitled "A Review and Prospect of China's Trademark Administration." The article is more than 10,000 words long and covers the history of China's trademark administration since the late Qing Dynasty, the drafting of regulations, the exchanges with foreign consuls, and the relationship with various commercial treaties. It can be regarded as a history of trademark in China. He also put forward several suggestions for the future development of trademark administration.

Petition to the National Goods Promotion Association for Tax Exemption: Mao Lee Button Factory's Products Complete Tax Payment 183

The Shanghai Citizens' National Goods Promotion Association stated that the No. 1 Manufacturing Plant of their factory member, Mao Lee Button Factory Co., Ltd., is located in Hankou. The semi-finished products are transported to Shanghai and sold abroad, requiring two tax payments, which creates a heavy burden. Yesterday, they specifically petitioned the Ministries of Industry and Finance, requesting tax exemption based on the precedents of European and American countries, to implement relief. The original petition is recorded as follows: A petition for a request: It is reported that our association member, Mao Lee Button Factory, stated in a letter: "Our country's manufactured buttons are exported and sold domestically and abroad. The increase in import taxes by European and American countries has greatly impacted our business, resulting in losses. The member's semi-finished product factory is located in Hankou. Its products are shipped to Shanghai, where taxes are paid according to regulations. Then, when shipped abroad, taxes must be paid again. Paying taxes twice on the same item creates a heavy burden and increases costs, making it difficult to compete with foreign goods. It has been found that semi-finished products are not taxed in European, American, and Japanese countries. Promoting sales is encouraged. National goods are in their infancy and in a state of economic downturn, making it difficult to sustain. Reluctantly, we request that your association petition the Ministries of Industry and Finance to approve a tax exemption for the member's semi-finished products shipped from Hankou to Shanghai and shipped abroad, in order to implement relief." Based on this, we hereby prepare this document and respectfully submit it to the ministries for review and approval, in accordance with the request. We request that the tax exemption for semi-finished buttons be approved, in order to maintain national goods and provide relief. We also hope for approval and adherence, which would be greatly appreciated.

Chinese and Western Commodity Trade Market: Discounted Prices at the Original Site of New World: The Chinese and Western Commodity Trade Market, held at the original site of New World, has seen participating manufacturers embracing a sacrificial spirit since the opening of the Chinese Commodity Department. They have specially reduced the prices of goods, which has been highly praised by customers. Among them, such as Shendehua's Industrial Society's Kangning Toothpaste is only sold for three cents per small tube, the Simen National Goods Company's poplin is sold at twelve cents per foot, buy one get one free, the Samsung Cotton Iron Factory's artistic pillows are only sold for ninety cents per pair, the Xinxing Pharmacy's Golden Dragon Supreme Oil is sold for one hundred cash per small package, and the China Oil Factory's soap is sold for eighty cash per piece, all of which are extremely cheap. There are many other factories with discounted goods, too numerous to mention.

Shenghuo Daily Products Cooperative Invents Fried Beans: The Shenghuo Food Cooperative, established by Mr. Lai Chengzhi and others from Xiaoshan, Tangjia Lane, 738 Tiantong Road, has recently invented paper-wrapped delicious salted fried beans and five-spice bamboo shoot cooked beans. They are baked using scientific methods, are nutritious, crispy, and beneficial to health, and can treat liver and stomach ailments. Currently, in order to expand business and solve unemployment, they plan to recruit vendors for wholesale sales. Those who are interested in selling only need one or two yuan of capital to solve their family's livelihood. Regardless of gender or age, they can serve as vendors at the cooperative.

Medical and Pharmaceutical Circles 186

Pingmin Nursing Home Adds Department for Epidemic Disease Diagnosis: The Pingmin Nursing Home at the intersection of Weihaiwei Road and Chongqing Road in this city was founded by Dr. Yang Shufu. Dr. Yang is an advanced figure in the medical community, specializing in internal medicine, venereal diseases, skin diseases, and smoking cessation, etc. His experience and knowledge are both extensive and rich. He has been practicing medicine for more than twenty years, saving countless lives. Therefore, prominent figures in Shanghai have presented him with plaques, praising his miraculous skills. His social admiration is such that the inland also knows that Mr. Yang has been managing epidemic hospitals in Hangzhou, Ningbo, and other places for many years, with outstanding achievements. Now that the summer season has arrived, epidemic diseases and digestive disorders are everywhere. In order to prevent this, Dean Yang has specially added an epidemic emergency department to the hospital, specializing in the treatment of various group diarrhea, vomiting, red and white dysentery, and other symptoms. The treatment is fully equipped with instruments and medicines, and a new ambulance has been purchased for the convenience of transporting patients at any time. Poor patients are treated free of charge, and free vaccinations are given. It is truly a blessing to society and a guiding light for patients.

Chinese Hospital Provides Medical Care: Shanghai philanthropists Du Yuesheng, Wang Yiting, Wang Xiaolai, Yu Qiaqing, Yuan Ludeng, Wang Binyan, Gu Shaoqing, Wang Boyuan, etc., in view of the proliferation of summer epidemics, and the risk of life due to carelessness, and the particular hardship of those who are unable to afford medical treatment, specially established the Chinese Hospital at 872 Beijing Road, Xizang Road, providing medical care day and night. If there are serious cases that require hospitalization, medical treatment, medicine, and hospitalization are all free of charge, and free vaccinations are provided. Recently, due to insufficient space at the hospital address for epidemic prevention work, the Chinese Epidemic Hospital was added at the intersection of Huade Road in Tilanqiao, which opened on the 10th of this month. Many famous Shanghai doctors have been hired to provide medical care day and night to benefit the common people. It is heard that those suffering from epidemics who seek treatment come in droves, averaging more than two hundred people per day.

Hongmiao Abbot Provides Medical Care: The abbot of Hongmiao Temple on Nanjing Road, Zhang Weixin, in view of the pity of the poor and sick, every summer, invites national physicians Hou Kangbo, Xi Shouren, and Hou Wenshou to the temple to provide medical treatment and medicine. With the assistance of Mr. Wang Wenmei, who has raised funds for medicines, medical treatment and medicine will be provided to poor and sick people for three months from 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM every day, from June 25th to September 30th, so that they can benefit from it.

Calligraphy and Painting News 187

Kuiwen Hall Correspondence Course in Traditional Chinese Painting Opens Evening Classes: The hall's correspondence course has been running for several years and has produced many talents. Now that the summer vacation has arrived, evening classes have been opened, divided into three subjects: figure painting, landscape painting, and flower and bird painting. Every Thursday, Cha Yingu teaches landscape painting; every Tuesday and Friday, Yao Hongzhao teaches flower and bird painting; every Wednesday and Saturday, Ren Yunfeng teaches figure painting. Classes are held from 8:00 PM to 10:00 PM every evening. The tuition fee is three yuan per subject, five yuan for two subjects, and six yuan for three subjects. Register as soon as possible.

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that Shandong and its surroundings are clear, with strong winds coming from the southeast to southwest. The middle and lower reaches of the Yangtze River are cloudy and hot, still sunny, with southeast to southwest winds. There is fog in the morning. The East Sea turns from clear to cloudy, with rain in several places. The southeast wind is quite strong. Taiwan and its surroundings have southeast to southwest winds. Also, within the 24 hours before 2:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 86.2, and the lowest was 72.1. On the same day last year, the highest was 102, and the lowest was 76.1.

Competition Committee of the National Games Passes General Order Table for the Conference 190

Athletics Schedule and Swimming Order Drafted and Passed: Ball Game Competition Passes Order Allocation Principles: Special Competition Rules are Specified to Facilitate the Competition

The Competition Committee of the Preparatory Committee for the Sixth National Games announced the minutes of the first meeting as follows:

Time: 3:00 PM on June 25th; Location: Conference Room of this Committee's Office; Attendees: Hao Gengsheng, Jiang Xiangqing, Chen Kuisheng (Jiang Xiangqing representing), Chu Minyi (Xu Zhiyi representing), Yuan Dunli, Gao Zi, Chen Yongsheng, Shen Guoquan, Wu Yunrui, Wang Fudan, Rong Qizhao, Shen Siliang, Wu Bangwei (Shen representing), Cheng Dengke (Wu representing), Wang Zhengting, Shao Rugan, Xu Ba (Xu Zhiyi representing); Observers: Xu Zhiyi, Zhou Jiaqi; Chairman: Wang Zhengting; Recorder: Wang Daxu; Opening Ceremony.

Report Items

A preparatory committee has been established to carry out preparatory matters. However, the most important part of the preparatory work is the competition part. Today is the first meeting after the establishment of the Competition Committee. In the future, we will rely on the efforts and support of all competition committee members. The National Arts Court will be set up inside the athletics competition venue. 5. It is suggested to the Conference Preparatory Committee.

Special Competition Regulations 191

Chapter I: General Principles

Article 1: The organizing committee, in order to ensure the orderly conduct of various sports competitions and to achieve perfect results, hereby establishes these regulations.

Article 2: All participating units, officials, and athletes must comply with the provisions of these regulations.

Article 3: If there are any omissions or necessary amendments to these regulations, the competition review committee of the organizing committee may supplement or revise and announce them at any time.

Chapter II: Track and Field

Article 4: Athlete number cloths must have all four sides securely sewn with needle and thread, one each on the chest and back. Those that are not properly sewn or are inappropriately positioned (such as on the waist of the trousers) may be stopped from competing by the venue manager.

Article 5: The times for all sports competitions are specified in detail in the schedule. Therefore, the reporting method will no longer be used during the competition. Athletes should pay attention to the starting time of their events and gather at the designated location on time.

Article 6: For careful consideration, the organizing committee will ring an electric bell once before the start of each event (this bell is installed in the athletes' lounge and on the field). Within five minutes after the bell stops ringing, gathering and roll call will begin at each designated location. If an athlete is absent for two roll calls, they will not be allowed to participate in that event and will be considered to have voluntarily forfeited. Time will be based on the standard clock provided by the organizing committee.

Article 7: After the roll call for field or track events, the field event recorder or track event registrar will lead the athletes into the field to begin the competition.

Article 8: Athletes participating in field events should sit in their designated areas while waiting for their turn to throw or jump. They may only stand up and perform appropriate warm-up activities when the referee calls their number and orders them to prepare.

Article 9: In field events involving throwing, the results of each athlete's throw will be marked with a numbered flag. The furthest throw will be measured. To save time and procedures, a standard line may be drawn at a reasonable distance. If many results do not reach this standard line or cross the line, the referees may, at their discretion, remove the flags for a portion of the weaker results. Athletes may not object.

Article 10: In field events where distance determines the winner, markers are placed at the locations of the Far Eastern, National, and World record distances to serve as targets.

Article 11: Except for the poles used in pole vaulting, all equipment for field events, such as javelins, discus, and shot puts, will be provided by the organizing committee. Athletes may not bring their own.

Article 12: For track events with preliminary heats, the groups will be predetermined by the competition committee.

Article 13: For track events with lane assignments, the order of athletes in each lane will be predetermined by the competition committee and listed in the schedule. Therefore, each athlete should remember their assigned lane number and take their position. The registrar will verify their positions. However, for track events of 800 meters or more, lane assignments will still be drawn on the spot.

Article 14: After crossing the finish line, track athletes should gradually stop within their respective lanes and not leave immediately to facilitate observation by the referees.

Article 15: Athletes in track events who need to wear outerwear after the race should hand it over to the Boy Scout designated by the organizing committee before the start of the race to carry it to the finish line. They may not have others carry it for them.

Article 16: After the finals of each track and field event, the participating athletes should wait briefly in front of the podium to hear the results. The top six finishers should immediately stand on the winners' podium in the order of their ranking to receive their medals and take a group photo.

Article 17: Except for the special circumstances in the previous article, athletes should leave the field immediately after each competition. Venue managers or security personnel may order athletes loitering or lingering in the field to leave. If they do not comply, their number cloths may be taken back, and their qualification to participate in track and field events thereafter may be revoked.

Chapter III: Combined Events

Article 18: Although there are regulations for the starting times of each event in the pentathlon and decathlon, the referees may order them to be held earlier if they deem it necessary. Therefore, athletes should not leave the field unnecessarily.

Article 19: For track events up to 400 meters, three athletes will be grouped together. For 1,500 meters, five athletes will be grouped together. However, the chief referee has the right to change or combine the groups.

Article 20: Athletes participating in the pentathlon and decathlon should rest in the designated area while waiting for their turn to compete and should not move around randomly to avoid disrupting order.

Article 21: For relay races, each unit should notify the registration and allocation division of the names and numbers of all team members and the order in which they will run by 5:00 PM the day before. They should then collect four markers and instruct each team member to wear them on their chest according to the order of running: A, B, C, D. If the order of runners is changed in the semi-finals or finals, notification should also be given in advance (for semi-finals and finals on the same day as the preliminary heats, notify the venue manager 30 minutes before the start; for semi-finals and finals held on the following day, notify the registration and allocation division by 5:00 PM the day before).

Article 22: The top six finishers in the pentathlon and decathlon, and the top six teams in the relay races, should wait briefly on the field after the end of the competition to hear the results, stand on the winners' podium in the order of their ranking, receive their medals, and take a group photo.

Chapter IV: Swimming

Article 23: Athlete number cloths must be sewn securely (see Article 4).

Article 24: The times for all sports competitions are specified in detail in the schedule. Athletes should attend on time and gather at the designated location (see Articles 5 and 6).

Article 25: After the finals of each event, the participating athletes should wait briefly on the field to hear the results. The top six finishers should stand on the winners' podium in the order of their ranking, receive their medals, and take a group photo.

Article 26: Except for special circumstances, athletes should leave the field immediately after each competition and return to the athletes' lounge. If they loiter or linger in the competition area, venue managers or security personnel may order them to leave. If they do not comply, their number cloths may be taken back, and their qualification to participate in swimming events thereafter may be revoked.

Chapter V: Ball Games

Article 27: For all ball games, the registration and allocation division will fill out competition notification slips and notify the head instructor or manager of each unit by 9:00 PM the day before to allow for preparation. If there is a discrepancy between the notification slip and the original schedule, the notification slip shall prevail.

Article 28: A competition record slip is attached to the notification. Each unit should fill out the names of the starting players and substitutes clearly according to the format and write the unit name on the last line, signed by the instructor to indicate solemnity. This slip should be handed to the referee when attending the competition.

Article 29: Only the competing instructors, players, substitutes, and one support staff member are allowed to enter the field for each ball game on time.

Article 30: Teams entering the field (except for tennis) should hand the competition notification slip to the Boy Scout at the entrance, who will verify the number of people according to the competition record slip before allowing them in. If someone needs to leave the field for any reason, they should inform the Boy Scout when exiting to avoid difficulties when re-entering the field.

Article 31: Only the players participating in the tennis match and their instructor or manager are allowed to enter the tennis court. Substitutes from the team are also not allowed to enter the court.

Article 32: If another team is already playing on the field for a ball game, the arriving team is only allowed to enter the field within 30 minutes before the scheduled start time. They should not enter too early and should leave the field immediately after the competition to facilitate the progress of other matches.

Article 33: All players must wear numbers (except for tennis). Those without numbers will not be allowed to participate in the competition.

Article 34: If the two competing teams have the same jersey color, one of the teams should change into a different color jersey provided by the organizing committee to avoid confusion. Which team changes jerseys will be determined by the drawing of lots during the selection of orientation. The team that draws the losing lot will change jerseys.

Article 35: The referees hired by the organizing committee will be fully responsible for recording and timing all ball games. Each unit does not need to send additional personnel to assist.

Article 36: The organizing committee has prepared special seats for the officials and substitutes of each unit inside the field. Therefore, everyone should sit and watch in the designated resting area and not move around arbitrarily in the field.

Article 37: These regulations shall be implemented upon approval by the competition committee of the organizing committee.

Principles for Allocating the Order of Ball Games 192

The appropriate allocation of the order of ball games in this conference is closely related to the second, third, and fourth place finishes in various ball game championships. It is necessary to gather the opinions of all committee members and make appropriate allocations to benefit from collective wisdom and avoid any potential omissions. The following are some proposed principles for discussion so that the work of this section can have a basis for the future and avoid unexpected problems.

(1) Each committee member should, based on their personal opinion, select eight units with the best performance in each ball game championship and submit a list, signed and sealed, to this section by September 10th, according to their ideal order (the form will be issued by the conference).

(2) This section will summarize the results selected by each committee member and present the eight units with the most votes as a preparation for the seeding method.

(3) Among these eight units, the four units with more votes will be selected and randomly placed in the upper and lower sections of the draw, and the remaining four units will be drawn and arranged in the different sections using the same method (the above three items may also be handled by a competition committee designating five sub-groups, each headed by seven committee members, which is also acceptable).

(4) If there are units with the same number of votes, the order in the ideal list established by each committee member will be used as the standard for separate stages.

(5) According to the above rules, those who ideally obtain the right to the semi-finals have been completely arranged so that they will not meet in the first round of the competition. Then, the remaining units will be drawn and placed in the empty positions in the overall order.

(6) For the tennis match order, each unit will place one person each in the upper and lower sections of the draw, which will be determined by lottery. The allocation methods for the upper and lower sections of the singles matches and the distribution of doubles matches are exactly the same.

(7) If there are special circumstances, they will be submitted to the committee for joint decision at any time.

Walton Cup Finals Day 1: St. John's Defeats Jiaotong 3-2, Aurora College vs. Jiaotong Today 193

The results of the six-university Walton Cup tennis competition show that Aurora College, Jiaotong University, and St. John's University have all won four times and lost once, resulting in a tie among the three teams. Therefore, at 2:00 PM on the 26th, St. John's first played against Jiaotong in the circular final at the Aurora College court. Guangdong vs. Marines Swimming Match Tonight at 8:00 PM at the Lyceum Theater Swimming Pool 194

The Guangdong swimming team, a well-known swimming powerhouse in Shanghai, will compete against the Marines team, a well-known Western team in Shanghai, at the Lyceum Theater Swimming Pool (i.e., the Lyceum Theater) at 8:00 PM tonight in an international friendly competition. There are eight events. Scoring will be based on a 5-3-1 system. However, for the relay event, because there are only two teams competing, the winner will receive all six points, and the loser will receive zero points. Tickets will be priced at 40 cents each, according to the Lyceum Theater's practice, to limit attendance. Guangdong team members must gather at the team's location at 1346 North Sichuan Road before 7:00 PM and take a special car to depart.

Education News

Ministry of Education to Establish a Dental College Starting Next Year 196

Approved Funding of Over 160,000 Yuan, To be Affiliated with Central University's Medical School

(Nanjing, 27th Dispatch) The Ministry of Education, noting the current lack of specialized dental colleges in the country, will establish such a college starting in the 24th year of the Republic. The central government has approved the required funding, with an establishment fee of 80,000 yuan and recurring expenses of 84,000 yuan. The Ministry has now decided to affiliate this specialized college with Central University's Medical School and has instructed the school to plan for its establishment.

Ministry of Education Promulgates a Provisional Vocabulary for Primary School Grading 197

Textbook Editors Should Adopt Accordingly

(Nanjing, 27th Dispatch) The Ministry of Education has compiled a provisional vocabulary for primary school grading and issued an order on the 27th to distribute it to education departments and bureaus in various provinces and cities and to major bookstores. In the future, elementary schools and bookstores should all use the words compiled for the corresponding grades in this vocabulary when editing textbooks and reading materials.

Ministry of Education Interprets Qualifications for Elementary School Teacher Certification 198

The Ministry of Education previously responded to a request from the Henan Provincial Government, forwarded by the Provincial Department of Education, for an interpretation of the qualifications for elementary school teacher certification. The response stated that a university law degree does not meet the qualifications stipulated in Article 75 of the Elementary School Regulations and does not qualify one to serve as an elementary school principal. Furthermore, holding a university law degree and serving as a director of a mass education center for more than three years does not meet the qualifications stipulated in Clause 1 of Article 5 of the Provisional Regulations for Elementary School Teacher Certification and does not qualify one for certification without examination. Similarly, graduating from a secondary school or senior high school under the old system and serving as an elementary school teacher for less than one year does not meet the requirements of Clause 1 of Article 5 of the Provisional Regulations for Elementary School Teacher Certification and also does not qualify one for certification without examination. However, those with the above two qualifications may be certified through examination.

Physical Education Teacher Association Exam to Hold Makeup Practical Exam 199

Tomorrow at Jiaotong University

The physical education teacher training school practical exam in the city was held continuously from the 17th to the 20th of this month at Jiaotong University. Because some female students were unable to participate due to reasons, the Education Bureau decided to allow a makeup exam to be held at Jiaotong University on the 29th of this month. Students who have not participated in the practical exam must participate on time.

Jiangsu Province Changchun City Jiangning Junior High School 200

The preparations for the relocation of Jiangsu Provincial Nanjing High School to Zhenjiang are currently underway, and Niu Yongjian and others have been appointed as members of the relocation committee. As reported in yesterday's newspaper, it has been learned that the Provincial Department of Education, in order to facilitate the opportunity for students from various counties near Jiangning to enroll after the relocation of Nanjing High School to Zhenjiang, plans to add a provincial junior high school in Jiangning County. As for the funding for the establishment of the school, the provincial department is raising funds. Director Zhou of the Department of Education is also consulting with County Magistrate Mei of Jiangning Autonomous Experimental County on the establishment method. A preparatory committee will soon be organized to plan and carry out all matters.

Graduation Ceremonies at Various Schools 201

Shanghai Art College: This city's Shanghai Art College held a welcome ceremony for Principal Liu's return from abroad, as well as the 16th graduation ceremony of the new system and the first graduation ceremony of the affiliated Chengmei Middle School, yesterday morning at 10:00 AM in the Yi Hai Tang hall. Representatives from the City Party Headquarters Wang Longzhang, the City Education Bureau Nie Haifan, Chairman of the Board Cai Yuanpei, Principal Liu Haisu, Vice Principal Wang Jiyuan, as well as faculty, staff, students, and guests totaling over 500 people attended. After formal greetings, Vice Principal Wang delivered an opening speech and welcomed Principal Liu. Principal Liu then reported on his experiences in Europe. Afterwards, Chairman Cai Yuanpei presented diplomas to the college graduates, and Board Member Cao Qiming presented diplomas to the graduates of the affiliated Chengmei Middle School. Cai also delivered a speech filled with encouragement. Representatives from Party and government organizations and various board members then gave speeches. Guests Kong Keda and Si Xiaoru delivered speeches. Afterwards, a student representative gave a closing speech and the ceremony ended.

Shanghai University School of Commerce: The City Center campus of the Shanghai University School of Commerce held its graduation ceremony yesterday afternoon at 5:30 PM at the New Tian'an Church. Principal Liu presided over the ceremony and reported on the purpose of the meeting. Dean Zhu delivered a speech. Lin Kanghou and He Dehui were invited to speak on "A Review of Commercial Decline," after which diplomas were presented. That evening, the school also held an annual banquet at the Hong Kong Road Banking Club.

Soochow University: Since Principal Yang Yongqing of Soochow University in Suzhou went to the United States to lecture earlier this month, the school's affairs have been managed by Dean Pan Shenming, and everything remains as before. New professors for the next semester include Shen Qinglai, Si Shimisi, and Gu Yidong. The school will hold its graduation ceremony on the 29th of this month. This year's graduating class includes over 100 students from the departments of Arts, Science, and Law, and over 60 students from the middle school. The speaker will be Liu Zhanen, the principal of Shanghai University, who is also an alumnus of the school. Recognizing that the number of girls' high schools in the province is less than one-fifth of the number of boys' high schools, and to meet the need to provide girls with equal educational opportunities, the middle school will reduce the number of first-year male students to two classes starting in the fall semester, allocating one class to enroll female students, totaling 40 people. The male and female students will attend separate classes. New dormitories and gymnasiums for the female students are currently under construction and will be ready for use when school starts, it is said.

Huizhong Middle School: Huizhong Middle School in the west Douduo Bridge area of this city has been established for over 40 years and has been officially registered. Zhang Dongmin, a returned student with a bachelor's degree and former professor at Guanghua University, has been hired as the principal. Principal Zhang is a graduate of the school. This year's graduation ceremonies for the senior high, junior high, and affiliated elementary school will be held simultaneously on the 28th of this month. Dr. Ou Yuanhuai of Great China University has been specially invited to deliver a speech. The school will establish a summer tutoring program this year, with classes for senior high, junior high, and elementary school levels. Classes will start on July 7th, and both male and female students will be accepted. Boarding is available. Applications have been very enthusiastic recently.
